# Skyrim:Liar's Retreat

Liar's Retreat

**Liar's Retreat** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") and connected underground cellar northeast of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and invading [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). It contains only one zone, *[Liar's Retreat](#Liar.27s_Retreat)*.

Apparently, until very recently this used to be the site of a bandit bar run by a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") named [Rahd](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahd "Skyrim:Rahd"), who is known as "Longhammer" due to a unique weapon he carries. Falmer have tunneled in and are attacking the last of the occupants when you arrive for the first time.

## Related Quests

- **[Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat_(quest) "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat (quest)")**: Retrieve [the Longhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Longhammer "Skyrim:The Longhammer") from a fallen [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahd "Skyrim:Rahd").

### Exterior

The entrance is marked by a cairn. Just below the first cairn is a corundum ore vein. Two lit braziers are on either side of an unlocked wooden door that has been set into the rock face. There is a leveled beast that may attack you.

#### Dining Hall

Liar's Retreat interior

Upon entering, there are stairs descending to a balcony overlooking the main bar area. You'll witness a raid of Falmer finishing off the last of the bandit residents. Descend the stairs to the main bar area to find everything in an uproar. Overturned tables and chairs, the corpses of bandits, a burnt corpse in the fire to the left, and blood and gore everywhere show the ferocity of the attack. There are seven leveled Falmer, including two magic-users, in this area including one hidden in a bedroom and another in the kitchen, which can lead to a challenging fight for the unwary. The Falmer have tunneled their way from deeper nests which contain more Falmer, a [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") (replaced with a chaurus hunter if *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* is installed), and some [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider").

There are the bodies of six bandits including one that appears to be a bard still holding his [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") and one behind the bar that appears to be acting as a serving girl. Around the room are two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks, two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and pieces of cheese. Against the southeast wall is a food barrel. A [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe") has been chopped into the counter, while under it are a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), two leveled [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), and a leveled [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Behind the counter is a food barrel and along the rear wall are three sets of shelves and a cupboard. The cupboard only holds clutter, while the shelves hold two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a loaf of bread, two bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"), two food barrels, and two mead barrels, and hanging from one of the shelves is a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam").

#### Sleeping Quarters

From the northeast corridor you can hear a bandit that is still alive talking to himself. There are three bedrooms in this corridor; the first of these has a novice lock and has been barricaded by the bandit. He will immediately attack as soon as you open the door. The barricade is made up of many baskets and buckets. The room contains two unowned single beds, a table and chairs in the western corner, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") against the rear wall. A cupboard in the eastern corner holds a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a pair of random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), and a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). By the foot of one of the beds is a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), and one of the baskets contains a cabbage, a bulb of garlic, and a piece of bread. On the table are a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

The middle bedroom contains a Falmer, unless they joined the fight in the main bar area. It appears to be a communal room containing six beds, two of which are now unusable. The bodies of another three bandits can be found in this room, and along the rear wall are three bookcases containing seven common books, many [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), and on top of the last of these is a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide"). On the floor are another couple of common books and a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") as well as plenty of blood and gore. The last bedroom has also been partially trashed by the Falmer, with a bookcase knocked over and clutter spread over the floor with a couple of common books among the carnage. The room contains an unowned single bed in the eastern corner, an adept-locked chest against the rear wall, and a long wooden table by the door with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and three common books on top. At the foot of the bed is a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), and under it is a [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor"), which can be most easily retrieved with the use of [telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"). A stone shelf on the far side of the room holds a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Biography of the Wolf Queen](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_the_Wolf_Queen "Skyrim:Biography of the Wolf Queen")*, along with a helmet and several potions.

#### Kitchen

Behind the bar in the main room, a hole in the wall leads to the kitchen, where another Falmer waits unless it had also been alerted by the fighting. The kitchen area contains a sideboard against the northwest wall with a table beside it coming out from the wall. There are four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a random potion of healing, and a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") on top. Against the northeast wall is a large fireplace with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") in front, while on the right-hand side of the hearth are a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against a pile of firewood and a small coin purse hidden behind an empty bucket in the corner (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

Along the southeast wall are a sideboard with two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top and a set of shelves to the right holding two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a [spider egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), four [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), and another woodcutter's axe. In front of this on the floor is a cast iron pot containing a [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), two carrots, and a bulb of garlic. In the southern corner is a brewing vat with a cupboard and set of shelves to the right, along the southwest wall; they hold two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and some cheese. Overhead, hanging from two beams are three bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), four [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), a garlic braid, and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), while in the middle of the room is a table with a baked potato, a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a fillet of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), a piece of cheese, and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") on top. The kitchen also connects to the corridor with the three bedrooms via a wooden door in the northwest wall.

#### Spider Tunnels

Spider tunnels

Falmer tent

As you pass through the door to the northwest, you find the hole where the Falmer broke through to mount the attack; ahead is the fire from a dropped [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") beside the body of another dead bandit. The tunnel takes a couple turns and passes a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") growing on the wall, before opening out into a cavern covered with spiderwebs. There is a frostbite spider by the entrance, with a Falmer off to the right that will investigate any fighting. A couple more spiders may drop from the ceiling as well. Around the corner, to the southwest, is a Falmer tent containing an apprentice-locked Falmer chest and a random potion of healing. Next to this is a narrow tunnel that twists and turns with several [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Egg Sac"), numerous glowing mushrooms, and several types of fungi growing in patches throughout.

At the end of the tunnel is a leveled Falmer waiting on a ledge. Beyond is a ramp heading up and to the west, with a dormant Falmer hive on the wall to the right. There are two [corundom ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") at the base of the ramp. However, mining these before clearing the cave system will alert several Falmer and a bandit to your presence. There are a glowing mushroom, a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus, a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"), a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") scattered on the ground by the ore veins. As you climb the ramp there is a rock on the left, by a pillar, with a random potion of healing, two [skeever tails](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail"), a [Falmer ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), and another bleeding crown fungus on top. To the right is an unlocked Falmer chest with a random potion of healing beside it.

#### Chaurus Den

At the top of the ramp, the path descends again to the northwest to an area with a leveled Falmer and two pens. Each pen contains the body of a dead bandit, while the pen on the right also has two living bandits trapped inside who attempt to escape.

Altar with Rahd

As the path starts to rise to the north there is another leveled Falmer standing guard with two more nearby that can easily be alerted by any fighting. There is a third corundum ore vein on the left where the path turns to the east. As you descend there is some carved stonework on the left, and a Dwemer piston is pumping above. As the path turns back to the northeast, there is an open Falmer gate leading into a large circular cave, partially fenced in with Dwemer metal work. A leveled chaurus is off to the right, and a Falmer tent with a leveled Falmer standing inside is to the left. In the center of the room, on an altar, is Rahd's body. Next to him, or slightly underneath the altar, is [the Longhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Longhammer "Skyrim:The Longhammer"), a unique [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") notable for its 30% faster swing speed. In the rear are two more Falmer tents. An unlocked Dwemer chest is next to the tent on the left, hidden among some vegetation. The tent on the right has a Falmer bow on the ground. On the north wall, there is a flat rock with a [Falmer shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Shield "Skyrim:Falmer Shield"), a [Falmer bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Bow "Skyrim:Falmer Bow"), two skeever tails, and three glowing mushroom samples next to the body of a dead chaurus. There is an unlocked Falmer chest to the right with three loose [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") on the ground. Behind the Dwemer fence is an area full of chaurus egg sacs and the gory remains of a human. A ramp is also behind the fencing, leading up to a fourth Falmer tent.

There is no shortcut back to the bar, so you need to retrace your steps. When you leave the tunnels, returning to the bar area after clearing the cave, you will be confronted by some aggressive bandits that are just entering the bar. Among them is a bandit chief who remarks, *"Hey, Longhammer, set us up with a round of... what in Oblivion happened in here?"*, indicating Rahd was probably the barkeep of the establishment before the Falmer attack.

|  |
| --- |
| Fungi growing in the cave system (minimum figures):  - 6 Bleeding Crown - 2 Blisterwort - 3 Fly Amanita - 36 Glowing Mushroom - 6 Imp Stool - 13 Namira's Rot - 4 White Cap |

## Notes

- There is an additional corundum ore vein outside the cave to the south down the cliff.
- While the Falmer will respawn, the bandits may not. Occasionally, on return visits, bandits may be heard fighting Falmer deeper in the cave, and their corpses can be found as far in as the boss cave. Also, a live bandit may appear in the fenced-off area just before the final room, but they will only act as a generic enemy.
- Liar's Retreat and [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") are the only two places in the game where you can obtain the semi-rare [tavern clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000d191f "Skyrim:Clothing") without killing or stealing, as the outfit is not sold by any merchants.

## Bugs

- You may not be able to interact with the coin purse in the kitchen. However, if you are a crossbow user and have explosive bolts with you, firing any such bolt at the coin purse will cause it to vanish; it may often reappear (rather bizarrely) at the top of the steps leading up to the main entrance door of the dungeon. It can also appear randomly in any of the passages deeper in the dungeon.
- The Longhammer may be under the table, not on it. It also may have fallen off the table and be near the gate through which you entered the room.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If you clear the dungeon without taking the Longhammer, it will be repopulated with Falmer, but the warhammer and Rahd's body may be missing.
- If you grab the Longhammer without killing the Falmer boss (thus not clearing the dungeon), everything in the cave will respawn after a few days, including the Longhammer. This allows you to obtain multiple copies of the weapon as long the location is not marked as cleared. **?**

*"We'll drive out the Empire from this land that we own. With our blood and our steel we will take back our home."*

## Quick Walkthrough

Liberate each of Skyrim's [Holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") (depending upon your choices during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")):

1. Liberate [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
2. Liberate [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach").
3. Liberate [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch").
4. Liberate [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").
5. Liberate [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)").
6. Liberate [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").
7. Liberate [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar").

### Quest Options

This quest governs the overall progress of the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") for the Stormcloaks. It is completed by doing a series of other quests that are assigned to you as the Liberation of Skyrim progresses.

The overall goal of the quest is to conquer each hold of Skyrim, one at a time, by taking control of the [military fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") for each hold. The holds to be conquered are altered by negotiations during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"), and therefore there are many possible ways to complete this quest.

- Without doing Season Unending, only the Imperial-controlled holds in the following table need to be conquered.
- The Stormcloak-controlled holds only need to be conquered if given to the Imperials during Season Unending.
- The Imperial-controlled holds will not need to be conquered if taken from the Imperials during Season Unending.
- Also, if you do Season Unending, then this quest will be put on hold until you have completed the main quest. After you defeat Alduin, then you will be able to continue with this quest.

| Hold | Initial Allegiance | Stormcloak Camp | Quests |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | Stormcloaks | *None* | Always Stormcloak-controlled (if you have joined the Stormcloaks) |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | Neutral | [Whiterun Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Whiterun Stormcloak Camp") | Always becomes Stormcloak-controlled during the previous quest, [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | Imperial[[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Falkreath Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp") | - [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad") |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | Imperial [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Reach Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp") | - [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)") - [The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)") |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | Imperial [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp") | - [A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)") - [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)") |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | Stormcloaks [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp") | - [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)") |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | Stormcloaks [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp") | - [The Battle for Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Kastav") |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | Stormcloaks [[1]](#intnote_Treaty) | [Rift Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp") | - [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Stormcloaks)") |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | Imperial | [Haafingar Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp") | Haafingar is always the final hold that needs to be conquered.  - [The Battle for Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Hraggstad") - [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") |

[^1](#note_Treaty)These holds can change sides during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").

One final complication is that when you complete the quest [Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer") during the [Main Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Main_Quest "Skyrim:Main Quest"), any hold (other than Haafingar) that you have previously been tasked with liberating is immediately transferred to Stormcloak control. All remaining quests for that hold are skipped, and you need to return to Windhelm to receive the next assignment from Ulfric.

### General Information

In order to receive the next hold that needs to be liberated, you always start by talking to [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") at the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). Ulfric will acknowledge any progress you have made so far, including possibly giving you a new [title](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks#Titles "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") and/or reward. He will then tell you which hold needs to be conquered next, along with some explanation for why that hold is the next priority.

The next step is to travel to the Stormcloak Camp located in the targeted hold. The location of the camp has been added to your map, but normally it is an undiscovered location, meaning that you cannot fast travel to the camp. Once in the camp, you need to find [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist"), who is found in the main tent of the camp, poring over an updated map of the war's progress. Selecting the topic "Reporting in" causes Galmar to assign you a specific quest that needs to be completed.

In almost all cases, one required quest is "The Battle for <Alias=Fort>". The underlying quest for this battle is always the same, but is simply [radiantly](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") assigned to the [military fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") protecting the appropriate hold. In each case, you need to travel to the fort and help kill all Imperial soldiers present in the fort; your screen will update regularly with the fraction of soldiers who still need to be killed.

### Falkreath

:   *Falkreath Hold does not need to be liberated if it was given to the Stormcloaks during Season Unending*

Your first assignment in the Liberation of Skyrim is normally to liberate [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). In addition to telling you have free rein to kill [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") as you see fit, Ulfric tells you to report to [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") at the hidden [Stormcloak camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Falkreath Stormcloak Camp").

The only quest that needs to be completed in Falkreath Hold is [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad").

### The Reach

:   *The Reach does not need to be liberated if it was given to the Stormcloaks during Season Unending*

After you complete Rescue from Fort Neugrad, your journal will tell you to return to Ulfric, so head back to Windhelm and enter the Palace of the Kings. Talk to Ulfric and he will congratulate you, and give you the title "Bone Breaker" and a leveled weapon as well as the permission to buy a house in Windhelm. He will then tell you to head to the [Stormcloaks camp in the reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp"). Go to the camp, and enter the large tent and report in to Galmar, he says that the steward in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is secretly a [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") worshipper and you might be able to find some proof and then "convince" him to help the Stormcloaks. This starts the [Compelling Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Compelling_Tribute_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Compelling Tribute (Stormcloaks)") quest.

After completing Compelling Tribute, head back to Galmar, who will thank you and give you some leveled gold. Then report in to him and he will tell you that you are going to [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"), to take over it, he will tell you to go and meet the men preparing for the attack. This will start the next quest [The Battle for Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)").

### Hjaalmarch

:   *Hjaalmarch does not need to be liberated if it was given to the Stormcloaks during Season Unending*

After completing The Battle for Fort Sungard, return to Ulfric in Windhelm and speak to him. Ulfric thanks you for liberating the reach, and then gives you your new title of "Snow-Hammer" (unless you completed Season Unending) and a leveled shield. He then tells you to go to the [Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch Stormcloak Camp"). Head to the camp and report in to Galmar as usual, he will tell you that you have to deliver some false orders to the imperial legate in [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), but first you will have to get some orders to be forged. He says the inns at [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") and [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") are frequent stops for imperial couriers. This starts the next quest [A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)").

After Completing A False Front, return to Galmar at the Hjaalmarch camp and report in. He will congratulate you give you some leveled gold, he will then tell you to meet the men preparing to attack [Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk") and to take it over, this will start the quest [The Battle for Fort Snowhawk](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)").

### The Pale

:   *The Pale only needs to be liberated if it was given to the Imperials during Season Unending*

Ulfric will Give you the title "Snow-Hammer" and a leveled shield. He will tell you to go to the [Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp") to help reclaim The Pale, and he will tell you not to forget it's your fault the Imperials have control of The Pale. Head to the camp and speak to Galmar. Galmar will tell you to meet the Stormcloaks preparing for a attack on [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad"). This starts [The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)").

### The Rift

:   *The Rift only needs to be liberated if it was given to the Imperials during Season Unending*

Go to Windhelm and speak to Ulfric, he will tell you to go to their [Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Rift Stormcloak Camp") in The Rift and tells you that he holds you responsible for the situation. Head to the camp and speak to Galmar. He will tell you to meet the Stormcloaks preparing to attack [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall"). This starts [The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Stormcloaks)").

### Winterhold

:   *Winterhold only needs to be liberated if it was given to the Imperials during Season Unending*

Go to Windhelm and speak to Ulfric, he will tell you that while it may not have seemed that bad to give it up, he now has to waste troops on getting it back. He then sends you to the [Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp"). Head to the camp and speak with Galmar. He will tell you to meet the Stormcloaks preparing to attack [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav"). This starts [The Battle for Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Kastav").

### Haafingar

After completing the previous quests, return to the Palace of Kings in Windhelm and report your success to Ulfric. He will congratulate you and declare you ["Stormblade"](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks#Titles "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). He will give you a leveled Cuirass and a full suit of Stormcloak officer armor. He will then tell you that the Stormcloaks will take [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") soon, and that you should report to the [Haafingar Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp") for further orders.

Once you arrive, find Galmar as usual and report in, he will tell you to meet the soldiers preparing to attack [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") and to take the fort, this will start the quest [The Battle for Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Hraggstad").

After completing The Battle for Fort Hraggstad, return to Galmar at the camp for further orders, he will simply tell you that the Stormcloaks are taking the capital, and tell you to meet the brothers staging for the final attack. The [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") will initiate.

After the [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude"), Ulfric will give you a leveled sword (even if you didn't kill [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius")) and then ask you to stand at his side while he gives a speech to the men. Whether or not you accept, he will ask you to at least walk out with him. If you decide not to participate in the speech, Ulfric will go directly to thanking the soldiers.

In the speech Ulfric will mention you, then go on to thanking the soldiers for all that they have done. He will then declare that he cannot accept the title of high king, until the moot declares him such. A soldier will then yell, "What about Jarl [Elisif](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair")?" Ulfric will then ask her if she will forsake the Empire and swear loyalty to him. Elisif agrees, and Ulfric announces that she will remain Jarl of Solitude. After the speech Ulfric will turn to Galmar and ask how he did, and after some talking Ulfric will thank you and leave with Galmar.

## Notes

- This quest and [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") are different radiant versions of the same quest. However, Liberation of Skyrim has more options because you may have been on either the Imperial or Stormcloak side during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending").

## Bugs

- Sometimes you cannot say *"Reporting in."* to Galmar at the Stormcloak camps and therefore cannot advance the quest.
  - Simply reload a previous save. If that doesn't work, attack him until he collapses, then sheathe your weapons. This may work, although you will get a bounty.
    - After attacking Galmar Stone-Fist, he may start attacking you on sight and cannot be spoken to.
  - Move to another location, rest/wait until the camp respawns (10 days) and return. See [Skyrim:Respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning").
  - By using "SetKeywordDataForLocation 16772 CWOwner 2" will force the dialogue to appear
  - Entering Pelagia Farm can sometimes fix the issue
  -  Entering this code into the console fixes this glitch and causes the dialogue option to immediately appear: `movetoqt CWObj`
  -  Open the console and write `setstage CWMission04 10` to begin the Falkreath quest.
  - Starting [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") may make this issue unsolvable.
- Sometimes when trying to report to Ulfric Stormcloak, you are unable to talk to him and can't advance further in the quest.
  - If this occurs immediately following the Battle for Whiterun, try the bug fixes [there](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks)#Incomplete_Bug "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)") first, as they will typically fix this quest along with other issues.
  - Move to another location, rest/wait until the Palace of the kings respawns (10 days) and return. See [Skyrim:Respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning").
  -  Use the console to select Ulfric (or use `prid 1b131`), then `disable` and `enable` him.
  -  Use the console command `SetKeywordDataForLocation 16772 CWOwner 2`.
  -  Failing all of the above, you can use the console command `setstage CW 4` to skip the dialogue and move on to the next stage of the quest.
- After the quest has been completed and Ulfric has given his final speech, Elisif may not be available in the Blue Palace. If you have a quest that has her as its target, the target will appear on the world map in Whiterun hold, but pathfinding will indicate that she is in Solitude. This blocks several quests from working properly. **?**
  - Completing [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") after this quest moves Elisif to the Blue Palace.
- The "Liberate Haafinger" and "Report to Ulfric Stormcloak" objectives will not be marked as completed in the quest log once the quest is complete.
- Ulfric was intended to be unwilling to start the attack on Solitude if the Emperor is visiting Skyrim. *"We're ready to march on Solitude, but the Emperor's visiting! The goddamned Emperor! And, as much as I'd like to kill the man myself, we can't risk an all out war with the Empire. We'll bide our time for now..."* However, this will not function because it reacts to [Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death") rather than [To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire"). This won't cause a conflict, as Galmar's failsafe works properly with the correct reference. **?**

## Quest Stages

Only stages and objectives relevant to the Liberation of Skyrim (rather than Reunification of Skyrim) are included in the table.

| <Alias=QuestNameLocation> (CWObj) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | I will help Ulfric Stormcloak liberate Skyrim from Imperial control. |
|  |  | *(Displayed as needed)* *Objective 1002:* Report to Ulfric Stormcloak |
|  |  | *(Displayed as each hold becomes the new target)* *Objective 102:* Liberate Haafingar  *Objective 202:* Liberate the Reach  *Objective 302:* Liberate Hjaalmarch  *Objective 402:* Liberate Whiterun Hold  *Objective 502:* Liberate Falkreath Hold  *Objective 602:* Liberate the Pale  *Objective 702:* Liberate Winterhold Hold  *Objective 902:* Liberate the Rift |
| 255 | ☑ | We have won the war by taking Solitude and killing General Tullius, and have liberated Skyrim from Imperial control. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CWObj stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CWObj`.

# Skyrim:Lifting the Shroud

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Investigate the haunted [barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow") outside of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm") |
| Location(s): | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow") |
| Reward: | [Sapphire Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Sapphire Dragon Claw"), Word for the [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") shout |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm")) |
| ID: | FreeformIvarstead01 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

Could the barrow really be haunted?

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Offer to investigate [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow") after [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm") complains it might be haunted.
2. Explore the barrow and track down the "ghost."
3. Take [Wyndelius](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius_Gatharian "Skyrim:Wyndelius Gatharian")' [diary](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Wyndelius's Journal") to Wilhelm for your reward.

### A Haunted Barrow

When visiting [Vilemyr Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilemyr_Inn "Skyrim:Vilemyr Inn") in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") you may overhear the innkeeper, [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm"), warning [Lynly Star-Sung](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynly_Star-Sung "Skyrim:Lynly Star-Sung") about a ghost in the nearby barrow. If you are intrigued and like a good ghost story, Wilhelm will inform you that [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow"), an ancient Nord crypt just outside of town, is haunted and warns you away from it as well. When pressed further, Wilhelm will confess to seeing the spirit and complain that the haunting is harming his business. If you volunteer to investigate the haunting, Wilhelm will think you daft and tell you of [Wyndelius Gatharian](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius_Gatharian "Skyrim:Wyndelius Gatharian"), an adventurer who went to explore the barrow a year ago. Screams were heard in the night, and the adventurer was never seen again. Alternatively, you can go directly to the barrow without speaking to Wilhelm beforehand.

### Ghost Hunting

Enter the barrow. At the first intersection, you might see Wyndelius' ghost through a locked gate to your right, asking you to leave. The first part of the barrow has no enemies, only several traps that you must navigate through. Head left to a room with four levers and pull the two middle levers (the ones closest to the door) to open the two metal gates. The right side lever triggers an arrow trap.
In the next room, to the right is an apprentice-locked door. Directly behind it is a pressure plate that activates a spike trap. It is, however, nowhere near the pressure plate so walking slowly over it will leave you unharmed. Beyond the spike trap is a booby-trapped chest. Moving back, pull the chain to open the next gate and continue on. There is a spike trap here too, but once again moving slowly over it will work.
Eventually, behind an unlocked door, you will find Wyndelius.

### Philter of the Phantom

Wyndelius will attack you on sight, unless he is sleeping, which allows you to perform a sneak attack or a stealthy inspection of the room. If you kill him, his ruse is revealed; he is not a ghost at all, and his spectral appearance was due to a potion called [Philter of the Phantom](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_the_Phantom "Skyrim:Philter of the Phantom"). On the table you will find his [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Wyndelius's Journal"), which explains why he pretended to be a ghost. However, killing Wyndelius is not necessary to complete the quest; you need only recover the journal. Take the journal to Wilhelm and, in exchange, he will reward you with the [sapphire dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Sapphire Dragon Claw"), the very item Wyndelius gave his sanity and life to possess. The claw is needed to explore the rest of the barrow, which contains a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") with a part of [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") shout.

## Notes

- The claw will be marked as a quest item until the player clears the barrow.
- If the barrow is left alone long enough to reset, Wyndelius' body will remain dead while replenishing a new bottle of Philter of the Phantom.
- If you pick up the journal before speaking to Wilhelm, you'll instead be given the option to say "Actually, you need to take a look at this." and give him the journal. The quest will still proceed as normal.
- After you finish the quest, Wilhelm will occasionally say *"Now that our "ghost" has been unmasked, I hope we see more visitors in town than just the occasional pilgrim."* when you talk to him.

## Bugs

- If the puzzle door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- The sapphire dragon claw may still be marked as a quest item after you finish the quest, which prevents you from removing it from your inventory. **?**
  - Re-visiting Shroud Hearth Barrow after it has respawned, and clearing it again, may remove the quest item marking from the claw.
- If [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") is used during the fight with Wyndelius, his journal may be knocked off the table and impossible to find, making the quest impossible to complete. Obtaining the journal and the claw through [console commands](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") will not make the quest continue, and the quest will remain unfinished even if you clear the entire barrow. **?**
- Even after you finish the quest and solve the mystery of the ghost, Wilhelm and Lynly will still engage in conversation and act if the ghost still exists, causing him to tell her to stay away from the barrow. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Lifting the Shroud (FreeformIvarstead01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Investigate Shroud Hearth Barrow |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Bring Wyndelius's Journal to Wilhelm |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformIvarstead01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformIvarstead01`.

# Skyrim:Lights Out!

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") |
| Location(s): | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse"), [Wreck of the Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner"), [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") |
| Reward: | Random loot |
| ID: | MS07 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| Difficulty: | Easy or Medium |

Extinguish the fire!

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").
2. Extinguish the beacon of the [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse").
3. Return to Jaree-Ra.
4. Head to the [Wreck of the Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner").
5. Deal with the [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder").
6. Clear [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Jaree-Ra waiting for you at the docks

### A Quiet Word

In [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), find an Argonian named [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") leaning against a wall under the stairs closest to the gate. Speak to him, and he asks how you would like making some gold. He then (if you indicate interest) tasks you to put out the fire in the [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse"). A ship called the Icerunner is due to soon come into port, and without the lighthouse fire to guide it, it will crash on the rocks. This leaves it open to be plundered. Jaree-Ra assures you that the men aboard won't be harmed, and 'may even be grateful for the daring rescue we'll perform'. After you agree to snuff the fire, he tells you to meet him again by the Solitude docks. He also warns you to not speak with him beforehand, lest you arouse suspicion.

### Professional Wrecking

Head northeast to the Lighthouse. There should be no guards in the building, although you may see [Ma'zaka](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27zaka "Skyrim:Ma'zaka"). Once you make it to the top, activate the fire to put it out. Then travel back to the [Eastern Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") and find Jaree-Ra. He will tell you that the ship never made it to port, and to go and find the wreck on the north coast (it will be marked on your map). He says his sister [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja") is already aboard, and is waiting for your arrival.

### Plunder Away!

At the wreck of the Icerunner, you have two ways to proceed. The [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") will not be aggressive when you arrive and you can simply visit Deeja for your "reward". Or, you can begin slaying marauders.

1. If you decide to fight the marauders, simply kill everyone in sight; there are no Imperial officers or ship's crew left alive so you won't need to worry about bounty. Make your way to Deeja, kill her, and loot the [note from Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_From_Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Note From Jaree-Ra") that will start the next part of the quest. At this point, skip to the [Broken Oars, Broken Promises](#Broken_Oars.2C_Broken_Promises) part of the walkthrough.
2. If you decide to visit Deeja, one of the Blackblood Marauders will stop you and explain that Deeja is on board the ship, two levels down. A possible bug here means the gangway to walk onto the ship doesn't always appear *(see Bugs)*. Around the boat are various containers, mostly food items, with some locked Novice-level chests. The things washed up on shore, as well as on the ship, are regarded as the Blackblood's haul, so taking any of these counts as stealing.

Despite Jaree-Ra's words, the sailors aboard are all dead. [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja") is waiting down in the ship's hold. She will tell you that she was expecting you, and that you'll get what you deserve. Speak to her, and she will explain that the plunder has already been moved, and that you need to be 'taken care of'. She will then turn hostile and attack; kill her, and then loot the body, retrieving a note from Jaree-Ra which explains that the plunder is at [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto"), and that Deeja should kill you once you've arrived. The rest of the Marauders will now turn hostile too; fight your way back to the top deck and make your escape.

### Broken Oars, Broken Promises

Once free of the ship, head to Broken Oar Grotto. In the cave is a network of scaffolding and wreckage. There are two Marauders at the top of the scaffold to the right. You can hear their conversation if you sneak up on them:

**Marauder #1**: *"You've been here for a while, right? What was it like back when we could still make runs out to the coast?"*
**Marauder #2**: *"Well, before that cave-in sealed our ships in here we could loot any size ship we wanted."*
**Marauder #1**: *"Where did you keep all that loot? I've been here almost a year and haven't seen any of it."*
**Marauder #2**: *"The Captain has it locked away in that drowned ship by his quarters. He says it's "to keep it safe" but I know he's just keeping it for himself."*
**Marauder #1**: *"If only we could get our hands on that treasure. We could get out of here and never look back."*
**Marauder #2**: *"Maybe. For now just lay low and do your job. I have a feeling we'll be rid of the Captain soon..."*

Once at the top of the scaffold, take care of the two Marauders, then follow the path up the slope. Continue along the ledge until you see the drawbridge, and take out the Marauder guarding it. Pull the lever to release the bridge and cross to the next ledge. The battle ahead will be quite tough, so it's a good idea to save beforehand.

You have two options to continue:

#### Follow the Left Path

Heading down the left-hand walkway (which is free of Marauders) will lead you around the cave and will end on a ledge overlooking the ship where Jaree-Ra is hiding. You can pick some of the enemies off from this spot with a bow or ranged magic; if not, release the drawbridge and continue across to the ship and deal with Jaree-Ra and his gang.

#### Into the Cave

Going into the cave on the right will bring you into the Marauder's living area, where there are two enemies but also loot. The cave comes out at roughly the same place as the walkway, but shows a path upwards towards the cave roof. A Marauder is keeping watch near the top of this path, so take care of him before proceeding to the peak. From here you have a good vantage point over the ship, and can take out more of the Marauders with arrows before they can reach you. Be aware that the path continues down to the ship on the other side, and that Marauders can easily run up behind you if you aren't careful. Defeat the marauders and kill Jaree-Ra. After Jaree-Ra is dead, loot his body and the nearby chest for a large amount of gold and various gems. The quest completes once you kill him. Additional loot can be found in the Icerunner Chest, which is located on the top deck of the shipwreck in the water.

## Notes

- If you have already cleared out Broken Oar Grotto previously, the inhabitants will not have respawned, and you only need to deal with Jaree-Ra.
- Should you sneak up undetected to Jaree-Ra and engage in conversation with him at the end of the quest, you will only get an ellipsis to respond. This is because there is actually no player dialogue response present at all in the game files, so the game fills the blank space with the ellipsis.
- This quest originally had a scenario where you could help [Ma'zaka](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27zaka "Skyrim:Ma'zaka") and [Captain Aldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Aldis "Skyrim:Captain Aldis") get rid of the Blackblood Marauders. In this scenario, Aldis would help you defeat the marauders at the Wreck of the Icerunner. The dialogue branch `MS07DeejaBleedout` and related dialogue for Aldis show that Deeja could be killed, but also spared. If she was spared, Aldis would make sure she got locked up. It's unknown what would've transpired afterwards.
- Once you extinguish the fire at the Solitude Lighthouse, the lighthouse will never be re-lit.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.4, fixes this bug.

## Bugs

- The gangway to climb aboard the Wreck of the Icerunner does not appear, making it impossible to get aboard the ship from the water.
  - Reloading or fast traveling to another place and then back again may fix this. You can also jump from the scaffolding to the prow of the ship.
- Deeja's corpse may disappear, making it impossible to get the note to continue the quest.
- If Captain Hargar falls into the water he will sometimes swim through the cave wall and disappear, this has no effect on the quest but makes the cave unclearable.
- It is possible that when you loot Deeja's body for the note about Jaree-Ra's whereabouts that the quest does not update and so will not add a quest marker.
  - Grabbing the note and placing it in your inventory, then reading the note may trigger the quest update.
  - If you simply travel to Broken Oar Grotto, find Jaree-Ra and kill him, the quest will be complete without all the objectives being completed.
- The quest that provides the tavern rumor about Jaree-Ra having a job for you is never terminated once this quest has begun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Despite Deeja and Jaree-Ra's hostility, they still count as "friends" after their deception is revealed. You can use that as a way to charge the [Ebony Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Blade "Skyrim:Ebony Blade").
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.

It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MS07`.

# Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet") |
| Location(s): | [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company") |
| Reward: | Leveled [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =2 ([Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet")) |
| ID: | FreeformMarkarthE |
| Difficulty: | Medium |

*"You aren't for hire, are you?"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet").
2. Retrieve [Lisbet's Dibella Statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Lisbet's Dibella Statue").
3. Return to Lisbet.

### An Empty Store

Near the market in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") is the general goods store, [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company"), where the proprietor [Lisbet](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet "Skyrim:Lisbet") is struggling to keep her business afloat. Not only did she lose her husband, Gunnar, in a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") attack, she also lost dozens of shipments to the Forsworn, including a precious, specially-made Statue of Dibella. She believes this statue would put the store back on its feet. When you speak with her, she is ashamed of the state of her shop and will then ask you a question: *"You aren't for hire, are you? A sellsword? I'll pay you if you can recover that statuette from the Forsworn."* Accept the task and she will promise you a great sum of gold for your efforts and the quest will be added to your journal.

### The Statue of Dibella

Once you have accepted Lisbet's request, your map marker will point you towards one of eight possible Forsworn hideouts, where you will find the [Lisbet's Dibella Statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Lisbet's Dibella Statue") in the location's boss chest:

| Possible Locations |
| --- |
| [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt"), [Bruca's Leap Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bruca%27s_Leap_Redoubt "Skyrim:Bruca's Leap Redoubt"), [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt"), [Dragon Bridge Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Overlook "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook"), [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt"), [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt"), [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt"), [Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt") |

Once you have claimed the statue, return to Lisbet in her store. When presented with the item, she is overjoyed, saying: *"Ah, there it is! This little gold delight is going to keep us afloat for a while. Thank you. Here's something for your hard work."* She will then hand you a leveled amount of gold as a reward.

### Reward

|  |
| --- |
| | Levels | Reward | | --- | --- | | 1–9 | 500 | | 10–19 | 750 | | 20–29 | 1,000 | | 30–39 | 1,250 | | 40+ | 1,500 | |

## Notes

- Oddly, you may be able to buy the statue back from her for *less* than your reward at any level.

## Bugs

- If you retrieve the statue after the completion of this quest, it will become stuck in your inventory as a quest item.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- You are prevented from starting this quest if you've already killed all enemies in the Forsworn camp before talking to Lisbet.
  -  Enter `setstage FreeformMarkarthE 12` to skip forward in the quest.
- In case Lisbet is killed before completing the quest, both statue and objective will get stuck.
  -  Enter `setstage FreeformMarkarthE 20` to manually complete the quest: you will receive the reward, and the statue will be removed from your inventory.

## Quest Stages

| --- | --- | --- |

| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Retrieve Lisbet's shipment from <Alias=ForswornCamp> |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Bring the Dibella Statue to Lisbet |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 12, 20.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformMarkarthE stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformMarkarthE`.

# Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **Find the Dark Brotherhood [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Olava the Feeble](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava_the_Feeble "Skyrim:Olava the Feeble") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt"), [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End") |
| Reward: | [Ancient Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Shrouded Armor") |
| ID: | DBOlavaReadingMiscObjective, DBOlavaReadingTreasureObjective |
| Suggested Level: | 14 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security") | | |

The Assassin of Old

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Olava the Feeble](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava_the_Feeble "Skyrim:Olava the Feeble").
2. Travel to [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt").
3. Make your way to [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End").
4. Discover a [Dark Brotherhood Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin") behind a hidden wall.
5. (Optional) Defeat the [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters#Hagraven "Skyrim:Monsters").

### The Reading

Upon successful completion of the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security"), [Gabriella](/wiki/Skyrim:Gabriella "Skyrim:Gabriella") will hand you [Olava's Token](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava%27s_Token "Skyrim:Olava's Token") as a special bonus, if you managed to slay [Gaius Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") in any hold capital. According to Gabriella, this is an opportunity not to be missed, so travel to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and locate the elderly seer [Olava the Feeble](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava_the_Feeble "Skyrim:Olava the Feeble"). She can usually be found relaxing on her porch behind [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome"). Show her the token and a surprised Olava will immediately realize why you are there and will then reluctantly provide a reading of your future. Along with some predictions about the Brotherhood, Olava will suddenly see a potential for adventure and wealth, a place hidden behind [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt"), namely [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End"). The last resting place for an assassin of old, his fortunes are yours to take. A map marker will be added and an exhausted Olava will send you away.

### Deepwood Redoubt

Like most other ruins in [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), Deepwood Redoubt is crawling with [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") enemies, so clear the exterior and enter. Watch out for the [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Traps") right after the first catacomb, then dodge the archery attacks from the Forsworn enemies overlooking the first chamber. Explore the stony steps to the right of the first set of stairs to find a dead adventurer and a locked chest. Move quickly through the southwestern tunnel, or an enemy may trigger the [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Traps") trap. Proceed to the first room and avoid the [elemental runes](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Elemental_Rune "Skyrim:Traps") on the floor. Taking the path to the right will lead to a pair of rooms with an Arcane Enchanter in one, and a Forsworn enemy in the other. A [Deepwood Redoubt Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt_Key "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt Key") is carried by the Forsworn, which unlocks the southeastern door in the room with the runes. Another trap awaits, so avoid the [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Traps"), kill the last Forsworn enemy and enter [Deepwood Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Vale "Skyrim:Deepwood Vale") through the door.

### Deepwood Vale

As suggested by the name, Deepwood Vale is an isolated outdoor valley, and can only be accessed through the previous cave. Follow the path down to the bridge and then if not attacked drop into the river and follow it right to an apprentice-locked chest and a Nirnroot at the end of the river. Also there is a sneaky master-locked side-door entrance at the base of the Southern right-hand side tower. After the unavoidable fight against another wave of Forsworn, explore the area for some minor loot inside the southern and northern towers, and a hidden area on top of the waterfall including an expert-locked chest and a pair of fixed [Predator's Grace](/wiki/Skyrim:Predator%27s_Grace "Skyrim:Predator's Grace") boots. There is also Quicksilver ore vein here. Finally, locate the entrance to [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End") and enter.

### Hag's End Horror

Immediately after opening the first iron door, you will encounter several hostile [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"), along with a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters#Hagraven "Skyrim:Monsters"). As soon as you attempt to fight the hagraven, she'll teleport herself deeper into the dungeon unless you kill her first, so there is not much to do but pick up the chase. Look to your left as you enter the room for an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a [Scroll of Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls#Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Scrolls"). Watch out for several traps in the tunnel ahead, then enter the next room for your second encounter with the hagraven and a few witches. Pick the fight, watch the hagraven disappear, then locate the handle behind the throne on the left hand side to lower the stone wall. Your target, the corpse of a [Dark Brotherhood Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin"), is hidden behind the wall. He is clad in a complete, unique set of [Ancient Shrouded Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Shrouded_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Shrouded Armor"), and by his side is an unlocked chest with leveled gold and loot. When you are done, locate the lever to lower the bridge.

### Finishing the Hag

Although optional, you may continue on to clear the ruin. Cross the bridge and check the left room for a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") and the quest-related book *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*. This room also contains a copy of the [Hag's End Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End_Key "Skyrim:Hag's End Key") which is easily missed on a small shelf to the right of the fireplace. This key unlocks the master-locked gate ahead, which contains a locked, trapped chest. Activate the nearby handle which will elevate three sets of gates and shoot spikes out of the wall. The hagraven is back in the next room, along with two witches and a huge [pool of oil](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Oil_Slicks.2FOil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Traps"). Dispose of the witches, attack the hagraven until she disappears, and pull the chain. This will close the path behind you, but open up for progress on the eastern wall. The next chamber is empty, but contains a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for part of the [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") shout. Finally, open the door for your final encounter with the hagraven, and your additional rewards.

You will find yourself at the very top of Deepwood Vale, with the hagraven waiting for you on a ledge. When you approach the nearby shrine, two leveled creatures will appear and attack. If you managed to kill her before she teleported, her corpse will appear on the ledge and no creatures will attack. Fight the opponents while dodging the [destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells from the hagraven. Use caution here as you could easily fall to the lower level and have to re-enter the door and work your way back up to the ledge. If you didn't grab the key from the Frostbite Spider room, the hagraven carries another copy. The unique dagger [Bloodthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthorn "Skyrim:Bloodthorn") can be found on the altar, and a boss-leveled chest sits to the left of the door you last came through.

## Notes

- The switch which lowers the stone wall to reveal the Assassin of Old will not appear on the wall behind the throne until you have received Olava's reading.
- You can keep Olava's Token if you drop it or put it in a container while she is still talking.
- It's possible to climb your way to the altar and pickup Bloodthorn before you enter Hag's End - from the secret area above the waterfall, work your way around the rocks.
- The hagraven's teleportation is scripted, and will always occur if you attempt to attack it using any means. However, it is possible to kill the hagraven before she teleports if wielding Mehrunes' Razor. If you manage to kill her before she teleports, she will appear dead at the top of Deepwood Vale.
- You can get the reading from Olava the Feeble at any time after completing Breaching Security, but the predictions will remain the same - even if you have completed the Dark Brotherhood questline and they have already happened.
- It is possible to obtain the Ancient Shrouded Armor without Olava's token if you've destroyed the Dark Brotherhood. Take [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") with you into Hag's End and during the fight with the first set of witches, she will resurrect the body of the [Dark Brotherhood Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin"), who will join you. When he turns to ash, loot the ash pile for the entire set of Ancient Shrouded Armor. Another option without Serana is to have [the Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") activated. In the room where the second encounter with the hagraven occurs, stand as close as possible to the stone wall behind the throne and active the power of The Ritual Stone. Exit the area and the corpse of the Dark Brotherhood Assassin will be reanimated and following you. Kill him and to loot the armor from the remains. Another version that doesn't require a Standing Stone power is simply to glitch through the sealed door via a plate pressed up against it and running against it or using Whirlwind Sprint. Once inside, grab his armor and the loot in the chest and then glitch back out via the same plate method.

## Bugs

- The Ancient Shrouded Cowl disappears and causes baldness when equipped by Khajiit or Argonians. The character's neck is also left glitched when the cowl is unequipped no matter what other head wear is used afterwards. After saving and restarting, the odd neck problem goes away.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- When wearing the cowl as a Khajiit or Argonian, a second helm can also be equipped at the same time for combined effects.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
- The assassin is not immune to reanimation, which can potentially cause this quest to break if his corpse is cleaned up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- On reaching the hidden room behind the throne the quest is completed, the assassin's corpse might not be present.
  -  You can summon a living version of the assassin to get his armor with `player.placeatme 0009d761` He will attack you though.
- Clearing out Hag's End and then starting this quest may cause the Dark Brotherhood Assassin's corpse to disappear.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
- The Ancient Shrouded Armor set can reappear on the body of The Assassin of Old if you reanimate him after changing location.
- The Word Wall may not trigger once you approach. See [this discussion](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Slow_Time#Second_word_wall_teaching_third_word "Skyrim talk:Slow Time") on the shout's page for details and possible workarounds.
- Olava's Token may not be removed from your inventory after the reading.

## Quest Stages

| Receive a Reading (DBOlavaReadingMiscObjective) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Receive a reading from Olava the Feeble |
| 200 | ☑ |  |
| Locate the Assassin of Old (DBOlavaReadingTreasureObjective) | | |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Locate the assassin of old |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DBOlavaReadingMiscObjective, DBOlavaReadingTreasureObjective stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DBOlavaReadingMiscObjective, DBOlavaReadingTreasureObjective`.
