Lod's house in Falkreath

**Lod's House** is the home of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath")'s [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith"), [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod").

Lod the blacksmith

Lod's house

It is almost always novice-locked and will require [stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") for entry. It's made up of two rooms: a living area and a basement. It is found near the center of Falkreath, between *[Gray Pine Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Pine_Goods "Skyrim:Gray Pine Goods")* and *[Grave Concoctions](/wiki/Skyrim:Grave_Concoctions "Skyrim:Grave Concoctions")*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") |

## Related Quests

- **[Lod's Lot](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod%27s_Lot "Skyrim:Lod's Lot")**: Buy a book from [Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod "Skyrim:Lod") for [Kust](/wiki/Skyrim:Kust "Skyrim:Kust"). ([unfinished](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests"))
- **[Some Light Theft](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")**: Do a favor by stealing an item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Speak to Lod](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_to_Lod "Skyrim:Speak to Lod")**: Help [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") reunite with his [master](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").

### Exterior

There is a raised, covered porch along the length of the front of the house with steps leading up to it. To the left of the house is a larger cover area where Lod plies his craft at his [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"). There are also a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). There are two more tanning racks in front, not under cover. Beside these is an open crate containing four [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). Around the house there are four [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and one [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"). Unlike most merchants Lod doesn't display any of his wares.

### Lod's House

Upon entering there is a long wooden table on the left against the north wall. On the table is a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). A basket on the floor to the right contains two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), with a set of shelves to the right of that. These hold two more leeks, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), with two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") and several pieces of cheese on top and two garlic braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging above. There is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel in the northeast corner, above the stairs leading down to the basement.

The stairs run along the east wall. Opposite the table on the south wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the mantel. There is an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") on the hearth. To the left, hanging from the ceiling, is a rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), and to the right is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). Next to the wardrobe is a round wooden table holding two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), and a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Some_Light_Theft "Skyrim:Some Light Theft")-related [private letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Private_Letter "Skyrim:Private Letter") is lying on the table next to his bed. In the southwestern corner and running along the west wall is a single owned bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot. To the right of the bed, against the west wall is a square wooden table and two chairs. On the table are five [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

In the basement, along the north wall are two long wooden tables. The first holds a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), while the second has a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of Nord mead, an iron dagger, an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") and a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), with a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") underneath. To the left is an end table and chair. On top of the end table are two [blacksmith's potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Blacksmith's Potion") and a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Light Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Light Armor Forging")*. Against the west wall is an unlocked chest, a wardrobe containing more clothes, and a couple of food barrels. Along the south wall is a wooden block with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top and a set of shelves holding nothing but clutter. To the left is a round wooden table and chair, with a loaf of bread on the table and a garlic braid, a bunch of elves ear and a bunch of frost mirriam hanging above.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Lod's [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). The items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") every two days.

## Bugs

- You cannot make an investment with Lod through the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") perk [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Loreius Farm

## Overview

|  |

Loreius Farm

**Loreius Farm** is a small farm in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), north of [Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower").

It is home to [Vantus Loreius](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius") and his wife, [Curwe](/wiki/Skyrim:Curwe "Skyrim:Curwe"). Like other farms, the farm can provide fresh produce, and you will not incur any bounties for harvesting the plants here.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Vantus Loreius](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius")  [Curwe](/wiki/Skyrim:Curwe "Skyrim:Curwe") |

## Related Quests

- **[Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial")**: Convince an unwilling [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius") to help fix a stranded [jester's](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") broken wagon wheel.

### Exterior

The farm is set back from the road with a path leading up to the single story farmhouse. The farm boasts a windmill that powers a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Grain_Mill "Skyrim:Grain Mill"). Behind this are two large fenced fields. The first one holds six bushels of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), fourteen [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants, sixteen [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and nine [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). The other is where the [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") live and where the [chicken nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") is located. There are several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks inside the mill and a couple of food barrels just outside the fields, by the fence. The front of the house has a fenced deck with a couple more barrels of foodstuffs at one end and a chair at the other. Around the farm are five [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") plants. The front door is novice-locked most of the time.

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 9 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  16 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  14 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato")  6 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 5 [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  2 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow")  1 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") | 1 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Loreius Farm

The house is a single-room dwelling with a set of shelves immediately on the left as you enter. These hold two leeks, a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, five potatoes, and four common books Several pieces of cheese, two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") lie on top of the shelves and three bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), two garlic braids and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hang from the ceiling above. To the right is a food barrel and coming out from the southeast wall is an owned double bed with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of it. A round wooden table sits to the right of the bed with two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a common book on top. Against the southwest wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and a hanging rack to the right holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

Opposite the door on the southwest wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand in front, while on the mantelpiece is a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"). To the right of the fireplace is a long wooden table and bench with two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two pine thrush eggs, a cabbage, several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a potato and a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") on top and a [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka") on the floor underneath. Finally, in the northern corner is a small square wooden table with two bottles of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on it.

## Notes

*"So many knife wounds."*

- If you head up the hill directly west of the farm, you will come across a small depression littered with the remains of slaughtered [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"). Two [poachers](/wiki/Skyrim:Poacher "Skyrim:Poacher") will watch your approach warily and attack if you get too close. [Vantus Loreius](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius") and his wife, [Curwe](/wiki/Skyrim:Curwe "Skyrim:Curwe"), may be overheard talking about it. Despite what they say, the boneyard is west of the farm, not northwest.
- If you turn in [Cicero](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") during [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial"), you'll be able to take things from the farmhouse for free without it being considered theft. Unfortunately, both farmers will dead by the time you return, and the guard who patrols the road will remark *"You don't want to go up there, citizen. It's a terrible sight. The farmer and his wife murdered in the middle of the night. So many knife wounds."*
  - If you turn in Cicero during Delayed Burial then wait too long to return to the farm, Vantus and Curwe's corpses won't be there.
- Unlike some other grain mills, the grain mill at this farm cannot be used to create a [sack of flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") if you have [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") installed, as it lacks an activator.
- Two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") can be found northeast of the farm.
- Although the owners here are farmers, you cannot [sell crops](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat") to them.

# Skyrim:Lost Echo Cave

## Overview

Lost Echo Cave

**Lost Echo Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). It contains only one zone, *[Lost Echo Cave](#Lost_Echo_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Double-Edged](/wiki/Skyrim:Double-Edged "Skyrim:Double-Edged")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Leather "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Leather"): Determine the fate of a Thalmor agent.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave is on the road west of [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") near where it turns to the south. Piles of stones mark stone steps from the road up to the entrance, which unusually for a cave, is a wooden door with lit candles on either side and a statue to the right.

### Lost Echo Cave

The ceremonial brazier

At first sight, the cave seems to consist of only two chambers. When entering, you pass through a narrow tunnel dimly lit by numerous [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") which leads to a misty chamber with a haunting aura. A large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") can be found within amidst scattered remains of clay containers. There a tunnel on the north side of the room that leads to the second chamber. Upon entering there is an altar on the eastern wall between two torches with numerous items including a random suit of [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), as well as three [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), the book *[Old Tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Tome "Skyrim:Old Tome")*, and a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1")*. In the rubble to the southwest behind the large pillar is a partially buried burial urn. Near the altar is also a ceremonial brazier, which can be activated by burning a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") in it. This opens a nearby hidden door. There are many mushrooms found growing on the cave walls throughout the cave system, as well as several [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") and a patch of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus growing in one of the tunnels.

Once you have opened the hidden door to the east, the tunnel leads to another chamber containing two leveled Falmer, at least one of which is a magic-user. The chamber contains two Falmer tents, and a fenced area with chaurus egg sacs and three loose [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"). One of the tents is on a ledge above you; to reach it, head towards the next passage, then turn left behind the large pillar on the left to find a ramp up. Inside the tent is a [Falmer weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Sword "Skyrim:Falmer Sword"), and to the right is a Falmer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). The other tent is to the right of the passage and has a gate. It contains four loose glowing mushrooms. To the right of this tent is a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein"); among the rocks to the right of the vein is an unlootable skeleton with a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). Along the next passage is a [Falmer nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Falmer_Nest "Skyrim:Traps") on the left-hand wall, which houses a Falmer that will jump out as you approach. Just after the nest is a side tunnel heading south.

Take care as you pass through the side tunnel, as there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") around a corner at the bottom of a slope that triggers a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap from the left. There is also a leveled magic-using Falmer. At the end, past an open gate, are the bodies of a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a [dead Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)"), with an unlocked Falmer chest beside them. Back in the main passage, there is another Falmer nest with a leveled Falmer inside. Around the next corner are two more nests, both containing Falmer. On the left is a brightly lit spot with rocks that can be climbed and a hole in the ceiling with some hanging moss growing; under this hole, on the rocks, is a large coin purse, a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), and a random [fortify skill](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Skill "Skyrim:Fortify Skill") potion.

The passage opens into the final area, where two chaurus, a leveled [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), and a leveled Falmer are all near each other, leading to another challenging fight. Once these enemies are dealt with, there are many chaurus egg sacs, a Falmer nest, and a tent with a gate containing an unlocked Falmer chest. There are plenty of human bones scattered around, and a satchel containing some minor loot lying next to the remains of a human rib cage along the western wall. To the left of the tent is a short tunnel with a handle on the left that opens another concealed door at the end, providing a shortcut back to the first chamber.

## Bugs

- Although Lost Echo Cave is geographically located within the borders of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), in the game data it is identified as being within [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). This means you may be sent here for Falkreath quests, but not for Haafingar quests.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- It is possible to enter the cave with the sliding rock doorways already open rather than closed, so when you offer the glowing mushroom in the ceremonial brazier, it results in the doors closing rather than opening. Subsequent reactivation of the ceremonial brazier will not cause the rock doors to open. If this happens, you will need to leave the cave and reenter. **?**

# Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout

## Overview

Lost Knife Hideout

**Lost Knife Hideout** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains two zones: *[Lost Knife Cave](#Lost_Knife_Cave)* and *[Lost Knife Hideout](#Lost_Knife_Hideout)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Blood in the Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_in_the_Water "Skyrim:Blood in the Water")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Headman%27s_Cleaver "Skyrim:Headman's Cleaver"): Deliver vengeance upon the enemies of the [Bloodfall Queen](/wiki/Lore:Bloodfall_Queen "Lore:Bloodfall Queen").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- **[Dungeon Delving (Bandits)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout.
- **[Dungeon Delving (Caves)](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave.
- **[Harsh Master](/wiki/Skyrim:Harsh_Master "Skyrim:Harsh Master")**: Take care of a runaway crew member.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader.
- **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Lost Knife Hideout is fairly easy to miss from a distance, but can be spotted by looking for the small waterfall-fed pond south of the road just southwest of [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"). The pond features two clusters of harvestable [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") (but no [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish")), and contains a selection of small fish used as [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") in [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"); the typical [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing") and [orange dartwings](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing") feed above the water. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is east of the pond, and a [beehive](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive "Skyrim:Beehive") and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") are near the path leading toward the cave to the west of the pond. A patch of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus grows to the left of the entrance, which is flanked by impaled corpses.

### Lost Knife Cave

The cave has a notable stream that runs throughout, which is fed by the pond outside. As you follow it downstream, you can hear two bandits talking about wrestling a [sabre cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat") that they have caged. They also mention that someone killed a [cave bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear "Skyrim:Cave Bear") with their bare hands. If you wait, one will leave and go on patrol; alternatively, you can just attack immediately. The archer carries the [Lost Knife cage key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Lost Knife Cage Key"), which open the cages they were referring to. They are standing by a campfire with stacked barrels on either side; some of these hold ingredients and others [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). Against the cave wall is a table holding a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and some bread and cheese. To the right is a barrel with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") on top. To the right are a pair of archery targets and to the left is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"). Before crossing the bridge to follow the stream, an iron ore vein is just past the watch post.

Follow the stream to a large cavern with an underground lake surrounding an island with two earthen bridges, one crossing from this side to the island and the other crossing from the island to the southwest. In the middle of the island is a rock pillar rising to support the roof high above. As you emerge into the large cavern, take care to avoid the [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging beneath some wooden scaffolding, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") lying on the ground beneath them. On the island are two bandits roaming over more scaffolding that surrounds this side of the pillar. High above you to the north is a wooden walkway hanging off the side of the cavern wall. The walkway descends ending on top of the scaffolding with the bone chimes under it. This is your exit route after traversing the whole of the cave system. There are two bandit archers patrolling this walkway and they will gladly join the fray if alerted to your presence. They'll either snipe you from above, or descend and tackle you face-to-face. You can wait until later to dispose of them if they are too difficult to kill with ranged attacks.

There is another bandit patrolling the bridge to the southwest, with another standing on a ledge high above the far end of the bridge and concealed behind a waterfall. On the upper level of the scaffolding is a table with a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*, a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and a single random [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") on top. The bandits apparently have set up a diving board from the lower platform. To reach this you pass to the right of the scaffolding before passing under the upper level. A short swim underwater to the south, beneath a waterfall leads to a small grotto containing an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a random [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), two food barrels, a piece of firewood and an iron ore vein. There are plenty of [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") to catch in the lake as well. A bandit may sometimes fall from the top walkway and pursue you while swimming, or if dead you're able to loot them in the water below. The ramp leading back out of the water starts beneath the diving board and circles around reaching the top immediately to the right of the southwestern bridge. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here; fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here.

The natural earthen bridge crosses to a wide passage, which continues to the southwest, passing a couple more bone chimes and a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers a [falling rocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap from above. It can be easily avoided even by [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"). The path switches back and rises, passing the chute for the boulders on the left. At the top is an intersection. Ahead the passage leads to the balcony seen previously overlooking the earthern bridge in the main chamber, while to the left and left again the path descends to a wooden walkway overlooking the switchback. A bandit will either be standing above the switchback or patrolling to/from a small room behind. There is a second bandit sitting at a table, on a raised wooden platform at the back of the room. There are numerous barrels stacked around the room, mostly of food. Under the table the bandit is sitting at is an unlocked chest. On the same table is a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and a single loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). The only other item of note in the room is an iron ore vein.

Heading toward the balcony overlooking the main chamber, you will pass a passage on your right. There is a stack of barrels by the edge of the balcony, with a random bow on top. One of the barrels holds ingredients. The passage on the right leads to *[Lost Knife Hideout](#Lost_Knife_Hideout)*.

Returning from *Lost Knife Hideout* through the shortcut brings you along a passage formed by the stream. Just before it falls down the cavernside there is a turning on the left. The walkway heads left and right in front of you. Any bandits not dealt with from below will still have to be faced. Heading to the right leads to a ledge where a campfire burns; nearby are two unowned bedrolls, an unlocked chest, two random [potions of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and a random [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons") sword. Following the walkway to the left leads down to a short drop and the exit.

### Lost Knife Hideout

The massive cavern

The hideout has been built into the buried ruins of an old fort. If you are detected entering the hideout, three bandits will attack you and a fourth may shoot at you from a walkway above. If [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), you can surprise the three bandits who are gathered in a room to the right. You pass through a hole in a wall to reach the room, which is laid out as a bar with a counter in the southern corner and tables to the northwest. In the northern corner is a long wooden table with an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") and a piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") on top. To the right is a barrel and a set of shelves holding two gourds, four [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs and another piece of firewood. Opposite the table is a cupboard with two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), several cheese wheels and two food sacks on the shelves. Hanging from the ceiling in this area are three racks holding three [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). There is a bottle of wine on the table two of the bandits were sitting at. Behind the counter is a rack holding three more rabbits and three more pheasants. There is also a set of shelves holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), five bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and four of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), with a woodcutter's axe, a bottle of wine and four more bottles of Nord mead on the counter. On the table opposite the counter is a bottle of wine and two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). To the right of the counter is a doorway through into a passageway with a T-junction ahead with stairs leading up to the left and down to the right and a cave-in. Among the rubble is an unlocked chest. At the junction, against the southwest wall are two sets of shelves holding a woodcutter's axe among items of clutter.

The stairs lead up to another junction, with another cave-in to the right and a small wooden table holding a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") skill book *[Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs")*, a potion of health and two bottles of wine in front. Straight ahead is a dead end with four unowned bedrolls and an unowned single bed. A bandit can be found sleeping on one of the bedrolls. There are two bottles of wine on the floor, one by the bed and another by one of the bedrolls. At the foot of the bed is a food barrel with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") beside it. In the southern corner is a small table holding a potion of minor healing, a bottle of wine and a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"). To the left the passage continues through a doorway into a room, which has had the wall opposite knocked out. There are several tables and chairs overturned and on the remaining upright table is a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and two bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"). Beside this is an archery target with several [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on the floor around it. Through the hole, wooden scaffolding has been built to form a bridge linking it to a passage opposite. As you cross, below you on the right is a corundum ore vein. Dropping down to mine it, you will discover an unlocked chest and two random potions of healing under the scaffolding. Follow the path down and back through the bar and around.

Crossing the scaffolding to the passage opposite, you will pass a waterfall on your left, which falls through a hole, before the passage opens up into a large chamber containing five cages, a fighting arena formed from wooden planking and one of the cages acting as the gate into it. There are five bandits found around the arena and the bandit leader who is locked in the arena and can be heard taunting the other bandits to come and fight him. Once all the other bandits are dealt with, depending on your level facing the bandit leader may be a very difficult chore. The easy strategy is to keep him locked in the pit and practice your [archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") or [destruction magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") on him. Summoning a creature into the pit is also a source of amusement. In the cages is the sabre cat you heard talk of earlier and a dead [wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"). All of the cages can be opened using the key carried by the archer near the entrance to the cave. On your left, immediately after the waterfall is an area containing an unlocked chest, a set of shelves holding eight [common books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Beside this is a long wooden table holding a leveled potion of healing, a leveled [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina") and a random sword. To the right is a food barrel and a second set of shelves holding eleven more common books, a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of wine and three food sacks. There is a ledge overlooking the arena to the northeast with several chairs along it.

To the southeast is an earthen ramp leading down to the caves and living area. Along the rear wall is a stack of crates with a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") beside them and a campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it. To the right of the fire is a boss level chest and a long wooden table holding a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), another copy of the Lost Knife cage key and a piece of cheese. Beyond this is a set of shelves holding a random potion of health, a random potion of healing, a cheese wheel and loaf of bread. By the cage that's acting as a gate is a table holding an iron mace, an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") and [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"). Between the cages heading northwest is a path that passes a string of bone chimes before heading up the stream caused by the waterfall to a master-locked chest and a corundum ore vein. You can drop down to this from the waterfall. To the right of the gate is a ramp and stairs leading up to a table and chair on top of the cage used by the bandits to view the action within the arena, and beyond this are more tables and chairs used for viewing. In the arena are several dead bandits, a dead cave bear, and in the southern corner a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"). The stream also passes through the arena before exiting in the eastern corner, under an unlocked gate. Following the path downstream leads to a shortcut back to *[Lost Knife Cave](#Lost_Knife_Cave)* and the walkway high on the cavern wall.

## Notes

- The expert-locked cages provide a good opportunity to increase your [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") skill. If you picked up the cage key earlier, make sure to drop it before attempting to open a cage.
- Lost Knife Hideout also appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online") as [Lost Knife Cave](/wiki/Online:Lost_Knife_Cave "Online:Lost Knife Cave").

# Skyrim:Lost Knowledge

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). Obtain lost knowledge

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") about finding more [Black Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)").
2. Go to the dungeon where the book is located.
3. Find the book in the dungeon.
4. Read the book and obtain its knowledge.
5. Return to Neloth.

### Neloth

*"Now, it's only a rumor of a whisper of a conjecture."*

After completing the quest [The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men"), Tel Mithryn master wizard [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") will ask you several questions regarding your encounter with [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora"). If you have yet to locate any [Black Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book (book)"), Neloth will finish his interrogation with an offer: *"Now all that's left are these Black Books, waiting for another ambitious fool to be lured into Hermaeus Mora's clutches. Speaking of which... I think I've located another book, if you're interested. Here, let me show you."* This will immediately start Lost Knowledge, a quest divided into three parts, but only if you have yet to discover the Black Books hidden in [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow"), [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike"), and [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine").

If you miss out on his first offer the first time, you can ask him if he has found other Black Books, to which the wizard will respond: *"Yes. Hermaeus Mora is devious, but then so am I. Now, it's only a rumor of a whisper of a conjecture. But I think this is the place. Now, hurry. That book might contain the final secrets of Xarxes, for all we know."* Every time you return to Neloth with a Black Book, he will make a copy and let you keep the original. The reward will always be a leveled amount of gold, and his special thanks: *"Excellent! I'll just make a copy for myself. It's far too dangerous to carry the real book around. Of course, I'm sure you can handle yourself. Of course you can. Of course. Now, take this for your efforts, and we'll call the matter closed."*

### White Ridge Barrow

[White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow")

[White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow") is an ancient [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") located in the snowy tundra of northern [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"), straight south from the [Mortrag Peak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mortrag_Peak "Skyrim:Mortrag Peak") landmark. Upon entering, you will find two bed rolls and two [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") lying in a pool of their own blood. Activate the door bar and open the wooden door and another dead reaver will fall into the room. Proceed down the tunnel and find more dead reavers, along with two dead [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"). Follow the circular path to the west and head down the spiral staircase. You will encounter more spiders, both albino and [flame cloaked spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Cloaked_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Flame Cloaked Spider (creature)") in what is seemingly a giant spider nest. Locate the woodworks to the east and a strange-looking [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), with a spider attached to the neck, will attack. Jump down into the room below and consider the northern path for a bit of extra loot and a fight against a boss-leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). Head north and fight yet another spider-infused bandit. Follow the northwestern tunnel and fight the spiders on your way. You will pass a chamber with two [ruby geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Geode "Skyrim:Ruby Geode") and a [heart stone deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit") and then reach the door to the next zone, [White Ridge Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Sanctum "Skyrim:White Ridge Sanctum").

The Sanctum kicks off with two dead draugr, and, behind the door, a huge chamber with several [jumping flame spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Jumping_Flame_Spider_(creature) "Skyrim:Jumping Flame Spider (creature)") along with even more odd bandits with spiders attached to the neck. You will also encounter [Merilar Rendas](/wiki/Skyrim:Merilar_Rendas "Skyrim:Merilar Rendas"), a hostile sorceress who will throw jumping flame spiders at you. Defeat her and investigate her body for some really useful items, including her [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Merilar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Merilar's Journal"), telling the tale of how she slowly turned insane on her [brother](/wiki/Skyrim:Servos_Rendas "Skyrim:Servos Rendas"), thinking he would take credit for discovering the spiders. She also carries a [cage door key](/wiki/Skyrim:Merilar%27s_Cage_Door_Key "Skyrim:Merilar's Cage Door Key"). Claim the key and locate the wooden stairs to the northeast. The room ahead is filled with spiders, so dispose of them and head up to the cage and unlock it. Inside, you will find Servos Rendas dead, carrying his journal. It describes how he, along with Merilar, discovered the mind-controlling spiders and how Merilar slowly went insane from the fumes caused by the experiments. The cell also hold the [spider experiment notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Experiment_Notes "Skyrim:Spider Experiment Notes"), with Servos' detailed recipes from creating special spiders from albino spiders, along with the device needed to create spiders (please see [this article](/wiki/Skyrim:Imbuing_Chamber "Skyrim:Imbuing Chamber") for details). The cage key also fits in the lock of the cobweb-covered door to the north, where you will find no less than four spider-controlled bandits behind a barricaded door, all of them obviously experimental subjects.

[Dukaan](/wiki/Skyrim:Dukaan_(creature) "Skyrim:Dukaan (creature)")

Return to the chamber where you met Merilar Rendas and head south. Remove the spider web and proceed through the tunnel into a huge chamber where the chanting from a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") can be found. As you approach the wall, the dragon priest [Dukaan](/wiki/Skyrim:Dukaan_(creature) "Skyrim:Dukaan (creature)") will burst out of his sarcophagus and attack. He uses a unique spell called [Frost Stream](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Frost_Stream&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Frost Stream (page does not exist)") and regular [Frost Cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Cloak "Skyrim:Frost Cloak") spells and can be a tough opponent. After the battle, claim his [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Dukaan_(item) "Skyrim:Dukaan (item)") and a boss-leveled amount of gold and go to the word wall and get a word for the [Cyclone](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyclone "Skyrim:Cyclone") shout and claim the contents of the boss chest. Lastly, a pedestal holds the target of the quest, the black book *[The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")*. Reading it will start the [black book quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)").

Once you return from the realm of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Lore:Hermaeus_Mora "Lore:Hermaeus Mora"), head back to the chamber with the caged and deceased Servos Rendas and follow the path leading northeast from the cage. You will come across a ladder and a locked trap door. Use the cage key to open it and you will emerge outside, in a small shack a good ways south of the initial entrance to White Ridge Barrow. Lastly, head back to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") for your reward and the next task, a trip to [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike").

### Benkongerike

[Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike")

[Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") is an icy [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch"). The exterior decorations reveal that the cave is inhabited by [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). Enter the cave and head down the slope and keep an eye out for a narrow tunnel to the right, leading to a locked chest with some minor loot. Before long you will arrive in a huge chamber where four rieklings will attack. Dispose of them and proceed in a southwestern direction where you will encounter a [bristleback](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback") and a riekling firing at you from a small tower. Take the southern tunnel and follow it until you reach a camp with three rieklings. Proceed forward and defeat two rieklings bursting out of [barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Barrel "Skyrim:Riekling Barrel") and locate the tunnel leading northeast and beware of the three [tripwires](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") triggering [claw traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw").

At this point you will arrive in a huge chamber, complete with an entire riekling village built upon pillars connected with hanging bridges. You will be attacked by numerous rieklings here so fight your way through them and stay on the bridges. Falling down can damage you, but will net you some additional treasure. After traversing the bridges, find the tunnel leading east. The surroundings will now resemble an ancient Nordic ruin, although three rieklings will burst out of their barrels and attack. After the battle, help yourself to some useful potions on the shelves, then enter [Benkongerike Great Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike_Great_Hall "Skyrim:Benkongerike Great Hall").

Rieklings on bristlebacks

The Great Hall starts with an empty room with some common books on shelves and a riekling tent filled to the brink with copies of both volumes of *[The Lusty Argonian Maid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid")*. Among the pile, there is a copy of the [*Spell Tome: Telekinesis*](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis"). Take the wooden spiral staircase upstairs and follow the corridor leading north. Behind the locked door is a boss-leveled chest, the [Benkongerike key](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike_Key "Skyrim:Benkongerike Key") on a pedestal, and a rare copy of *[Dragon Language: Myth no More](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Language:_Myth_no_More "Skyrim:Dragon Language: Myth no More")* on another pedestal. Take the path leading east until you reach a huge chamber filled with woodworks with several rieklings roaming around, some of them on the ground floor, others on the bridges above. You will also encounter a riekling riding a bristleback. Search the chamber for some treasure, including a [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") deposit, and head south towards the gate and a [rune totem puzzle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rune_Totems "Skyrim:Rune Totems"). Three of the rotating symbols have the correct symbol above them, so turn them appropriately. The last one (to the left of the gate) has no symbol, but the correct [symbol](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") is the whale. Head inside to a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") with a word for the [Cyclone](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyclone "Skyrim:Cyclone") shout and some boss-leveled treasure from the chest. Lastly, head east through the narrow tunnel until you land in a small room with the Black Book *[Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")*. Pick up the book and you will start the [Black Book quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)"). Once you have the book in your possession, find the door leading back to Benkongerike and return to Neloth for your reward and your next task, a trip through [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine").

### Raven Rock Mine

The third and final Black Book, *[The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")*, is found in the depths of [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine"). However, you will have to complete the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") to gain access to the book. Please see that article for a complete walkthrough.

## Notes

- This quest can be active at the same time as the radiant [Black Book quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book (quest)").
- As with [Find the Word of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power"), Lost Knowledge will not point you to every available Black Book. Several more exist throughout Solstheim that are quest-locked, such as the books located in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow") and the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak").

## Quest Stages

| Lost Knowledge (DLC2TTR1) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | Neloth has located another of Hermaeus Mora's Black Books in <Alias=Dungeon>. He intends to read it as soon as I bring it to him. *Objective 100:* Retrieve the Black Book |
| 200 |  | *Objective 200:* Talk to Neloth |
| 300 | ☑ | I retrieved one of Hermaeus Mora's Black Books from <Alias=Dungeon> for Neloth. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR1 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR1`.

# Skyrim:Lost Legacy

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Travel to [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb") and defeat [Vahlok the Jailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok_the_Jailor "Skyrim:Vahlok the Jailor").** |

|  |  |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim") | | |

The main chamber of [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Tharstan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
2. Travel to [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb") and talk to Tharstan again.
3. Explore Vahlok's Tomb and find the main burial chamber.
4. Defeat [Vahlok the Jailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok_the_Jailor "Skyrim:Vahlok the Jailor") and return to Tharstan.

### Tharstan

Tharstan packing for the trip

The small settlement of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") is inhabited by [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") living life the old way, with their own culture and religion, especially the worship of the [All-Maker](/wiki/Lore:All-Maker "Lore:All-Maker"). These welcoming and hospitable people let an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") historian and author named [Tharstan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan") live in the village so he could study and document the ancient [Skaal](/wiki/Lore:Skaal "Lore:Skaal") traditions. Using what he learned of Skaal culture, Tharstan wrote *[Children of the All-Maker](/wiki/Skyrim:Children_of_the_All-Maker "Skyrim:Children of the All-Maker")*, and the next book is nearly finished. He also married the Skaal leader [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice") and now lives in the largest building in town, the [Greathall](/wiki/Skyrim:Greathall "Skyrim:Greathall"). After your heroic rescue of [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") during the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim"), Tharstan will decide that you are the right person for a task he has in mind, and will actively seek you out when you next visit the village.

As it turns out, Tharstan is not only interested in Skaal traditions, but is equally interested in the many ancient ruins scattered all over [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), claiming to know most of them well enough to draw a detailed map from memory. However, his recent discovery has left him quite nervous about exploring by himself, so he wants you to accompany him as backup. According to Tharstan, a new passage was unveiled during an earthquake caused by the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain"). The passage revealed the entrance to [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb"). When you agree to go with him, Tharstan will run off to his temporary home, the Greathall, to pack for the trip, hoping you will meet him there as soon as possible.

### A Tomb Uncovered

*"A sacrifice will bring you closer to that which you seek."*

Vahlok's Tomb is located south-southeast from [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall"), directly east from [Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez"). Be sure to stock up on potions and have your best weapons on hand, then take the trip to the tomb. You will find the entrance located at the end of the passage caused by the earthquake. Head down the first tunnel and you will find Tharstan waiting for you. His fascination with the tomb is immediately apparent: *"Remarkable, isn't it? This tomb has been hidden for... well, who knows how long. Many centuries, I would think."* He will then proceed to offer you the first task: *"There are some sealed doors up ahead. Perhaps you can figure out how to get them open."* He will then guide you down a set of stairs and keep talking: *"I've had a look around and the only interesting thing I've found is this inscription here, and a switch below it."* When he arrives at the inscription and the switch he will continue: *"Now, I'm not sure if you can read the dragon language, but this seems to be a riddle of some sort. 'A sacrifice will bring you closer to that which you seek.' I wonder what it means."*

When you examine the room it soon becomes clear what needs to be done: dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") are scattered all around a gigantic burning hole in the floor, with only a grate to keep you from falling down. As per Tharstan's hint, drag (by holding down the "[Activate](/wiki/Skyrim:Controls#Activate "Skyrim:Controls")" button) one of the dead draugr onto the grate, then head back up on the podium and activate the handle underneath the inscription. This causes the grate to open and drop the draugr into the flames, acting as the sacrifice needed. While the draugr burns, two entrances in the room will open, one to the north and one to the south.

There is a chest in the water west of the cage along with two potions. Jump down in the water from the ledge nearby.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *"Perhaps they are connected somehow?"*  **Southern Gate** Head down the southern tunnel and open the iron door. This opens a path through the catacombs, where four leveled draugr enemies will rise and attack. If you are not carrying arrows, pick up a few from the draugr archer in this area; you will need them to solve a puzzle later. Head up the stairs to the east and activate the chain. When the door opens, you and Tharstan will arrive in a puzzle room with three pillars surrounding a large central pillar with different colored symbols. Tharstan will immediately head up to a plaque and start reading: *"Hm... three pillars. Other than that plaque, there doesn't seem to be anything else worthy of note. Let's see what the inscription says. 'All men must die, often by their own means.' Sounds rather grim, if you ask me."* He will then wander around the room, mumbling: *"They also have glowing stones of some kind at the top. They look vaguely similar to drawings I've seen of objects called Impact Stones."* To solve the puzzle, position yourself behind one of the three pillars and perform different attacks, related to the weapons placed on pedestals near the central pillar. Going counter clockwise from the plaque, use a melee attack for pillar one, an archery attack for pillar two, and a magic attack for pillar three. When all three pillars have been activated, the door to the north will open and provide access to the final chamber. Here, two draugr enemies will burst out of their sarcophagi, along with a boss-leveled draugr. After the battle, Tharstan will come rushing in and start to study the chamber, saying: *"These runes have faded a bit, but I believe I can translate the inscription. The writing describes a guardian who defeated someone named Miraak. In fact, if I'm reading this correctly, it says that Miraak was a traitor. Most interesting."* Once he is done, he will start looking for an exit, so make sure you loot the boss for the left part of the [Amethyst Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst_Claw,_Left_Half "Skyrim:Amethyst Claw, Left Half") and approach the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") for a word for the dragon shout [Battle Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_Fury "Skyrim:Battle Fury"). When you are finished, locate the open sarcophagus and follow the narrow tunnels back to the central chamber. | *"Continue along the path, don't tread where you've been.."*  *"This writing refers to a guardian who inspired both men and dragons."*  **Northern Gate** Head down the northern tunnel and unlock the minor loot chest in the alcove for a bit of treasure. Tharstan suspects that this room contains another puzzle: *"I expect there's another riddle in here, along with a puzzle. 'Continue along the path, don't tread where you've been..' Interesting..."* He will then look at the odd stone path in the center of the room and conclude: *"Well, I'm pretty sure about two things. One, the riddle is most likely referring to these flat square stones. And two, I'm not going anywhere near them."* With these words, he will find a safe spot and let you handle the rest. The puzzle is quite simple: just go from one square stone to the next, without ever touching one of them twice. Once all nine squares have been pressed down, the way to the final room will open. In there, four draugr enemies and a boss-leveled draugr will immediately attack you while Tharstan runs to safety. After the battle, the old scholar will return to the room and start his studies, saying *"Look! Here's another wall with dragon language inscriptions on it! Let's find out what's written here. This writing refers to a guardian who inspired both men and dragons. I wonder if the guardian was himself a man or a dragon?"* Loot the boss for the right half of the [Amethyst Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst_Claw,_Right_Half "Skyrim:Amethyst Claw, Right Half") and approach the word wall for a word for the dragon shout Battle Fury. Lastly, locate the open sarcophagus to the south and follow the narrow tunnels to a chain that, when activated, lowers a stone wall and provides a very quick shortcut back to the central chamber. |

### The Amethyst Claw

With the two parts of the Amethyst Claw in hand, it is time to unlock the odd cage in the central chamber. Insert the corresponding claws in the keyholes on each side of the stairs leading to the cage. When the cage opens, your elderly sidekick will jump into the cage and translate the plaque: *"Here's another riddle. 'Stay your course. To idle is to die.' Well, at least it's straightforward. There appears to be a switch of some kind here. I'll just stand over here while you flip that switch. I'm sure everything will be fine."* Flip the switch, and several magical platforms will start to emerge and disappear all over the watery area in the chamber, leading to an entrance far away. You will have to follow the platforms while they are present and be on the next platform before the former disappears. When you make it to the other side, the magical platforms will turn into a bridge and Tharstan will be able to join you.

### A Bridge Too Far

*"I'm glad these platforms appear once you finish them."*

Head through the corridor and face the next challenge: a gigantic chamber flooded with water and several [corrupted shades](/wiki/Skyrim:Corrupted_Shade "Skyrim:Corrupted Shade") lurking below. The drop is a very long one, but luckily a handle is present to create more magical bridges. Activate the handle and follow the bridge as it appears and disappears, landing you on a small alcove. Once again, the platforms will become permanent once you traversed them once, so Tharstan will soon follow, commenting on everything. Yet another magical bridge awaits, and its platforms disappear even faster than before. The last bridge leads to a huge iron door to the north. If you fall down you will not only suffer damage from the fall, but will have to deal with the corrupted shades and locate one of the various shortcuts back to the bridges above.

After the last bridge, Tharstan will open the gate leading to the ruins' Hall of Stories, excited as always: *"Ah, the Hall of Stories. These are found in many ancient Nord tombs. There must be hundreds of years of history etched in these walls. Too bad they seem to be too damaged to read."* He will then consider the [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Traps"): *"Hmm...looks like it needs some sort of key. Maybe those half claws you found would fit in here if you put them together?"* Naturally, he is correct, but the right combination is nowhere to be seen on the claw, so you will have to pay attention to Tharstan as he deciphers the writings on the walls: *"Perhaps there's enough undamaged text in these etchings to tell us the combination. Ah, yes, here's something. The first one has to do with a breeze, or maybe it's wind. The second one mentions the the*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *night sky, and the moon. And the third has something to do with fire. It also seems to mention scales."* He will then ask you to figure out the combination from these small tips. Turn the rings on the door to **Eagle—Wolf—Dragon** (In descending order, Eagle on the top, Dragon on the bottom) and insert the amethyst claw in the keyhole.

### Vahlok the Jailor

[Vahlok the Jailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok_the_Jailor "Skyrim:Vahlok the Jailor")

The puzzle door will lower to reveal a long staircase leading up to a chain that opens the way to the final chamber. The chamber itself is essentially one big trap, as almost all the tiles on the floor are [flame spout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap"). [Fire resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Resist Fire") and [Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward_(spells) "Skyrim:Ward (spells)") spells can be extremely useful here, so make sure you prepare before entering. You will not make it far into the room before the legendary dragon priest [Vahlok the Jailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok_the_Jailor "Skyrim:Vahlok the Jailor") bursts out of his sarcophagus and starts to throw high-level fire spells at you, so do your best to fight him and avoid the fire.

After the battle, old Tharstan will once again come out of hiding and start studying the word wall: *"Hmm, here's another mention of the guardian. I can only assume that this is the guardian's tomb we are standing in now. It says that he was loyal, and his reward was an honorable death. Quite fascinating."* Speak to Tharstan and he will further comment: *"How amazing! A real Dragon Priest! In all my years as a historian, I never thought I'd see anything like that. I suppose that was Vahlok. He must have had this entire place built for him so that he could maintain his vigil, even beyond death."* He will then reward you with 1000 gold and tell you that he will stay in the tomb a while longer, for further studying. Before leaving, make sure to loot the remains of Vahlok for a hefty amount of gold and search his boss-leveled chest. Learn the third and final word for the Battle Fury shout, then backtrack all the way to the entrance.

## Notes

- The book *[The Guardian and the Traitor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_and_the_Traitor "Skyrim:The Guardian and the Traitor")* details how Vahlok battled the traitor [Miraak](/wiki/Lore:Miraak "Lore:Miraak") back in ancient times, only to see him taken away by [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora") seconds before defeating him.
- If you attempt to read one of the engraved tablets before [Tharstan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan") interprets it for you, you will get a message that you can't understand it. After he reads each one, activating the tablet will show you the text that he read.
- It is possible for either you or Tharstan to fall into the fire pit and become stuck. This does not solve the puzzle, and since it does not cause damage, it can cause you to become permanently stuck, and so should be avoided.

## Bugs

- If the puzzle door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- Tharstan may fall off the magical bridge.
  - You can fix this by jumping down and opening the way for him to come back up.
  - Tharstan can be transported directly to the player's location via the console commands `prid xx018FD0` and `moveto player`.
- If Tharstan gets stuck and you reach the puzzle door ahead of him, or if he reaches the puzzle door and you're not with him, he will deliver his speech with the door hints, whether or not you're able to hear it, and he will never repeat it.
- The entrance to the tomb may still be covered when you arrive. If this occurs, fast traveling to the Skaal village and back seems to fix the issue. **?**
- If you activate the handle to start the first bridge before Tharstan reads the inscription, you won't be able to decrypt it. **?**

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 100, 300, 305, 310, 312, 313, 315, 320, 322, 323, 325, 330, 332, 333, 335, 340, 345, 401, 402, 500, 505, 510, 515, 520, 550, 600, 610, 620, 630, 701, 702, 703, 704.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2SV01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2SV01`.

# Skyrim:Lost Prospect Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Mine.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Mine.png) | Mine: Lost Prospect Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Prospect+Mine)) | | |

Lost Prospect Mine

**Lost Prospect Mine** is a small [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") east-northeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It contains only one zone, *[Lost Prospect Mine](#Lost_Prospect_Mine)*.

The mine is thought to be depleted, but careful exploration may be rewarding.

### Exterior

There are two sacks to the right of the entrance. To the left is a cart loaded with rocks with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") leaning against it and a [shovel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shovel "Skyrim:Shovel") next to a wooden crate.

### Lost Prospect Mine

Mine interior

The cave holds a wide array of mushrooms, with a total of four [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), ten [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), three [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), nine [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), nine [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and six [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"). From the entrance, the tunnel leads down, past a cart filled with rocks, a barrel, three sacks, and a lit brazier. The path then opens into a multi-leveled cave with a waterfall to the northwest. A table against the north wall holds a [miner's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Miner's Journal") that suggests the mine is likely tapped out and the previous owner, [Bern](/wiki/Skyrim:Bern "Skyrim:Bern"), disappeared without a trace. Also on the table is a random potion of healing and a sack. To the left of the table is a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") on the ground. To the right of the table is a ramp heading northeast; at the bottom of the ramp is a pickaxe. The tunnel heads back a few feet and ends; there is a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") on the floor. Back in the main cave, the next tunnel heads southeast down a short way to another dead end. Only mushrooms can be found here. In the main cave again, to the right of the previous tunnel are two sacks and barrels. To the right of these is the tunnel you entered through. There is a path heading west past two sacks. At the end of the tunnel there is a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") and sack, as well as a pickaxe in the southern corner. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, the shallow pool fed by the waterfall features a [tripod spiderfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripod_Spiderfish "Skyrim:Tripod Spiderfish"), and the table holds a [cooked tripod spiderfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Tripod_Spiderfish "Skyrim:Cooked Tripod Spiderfish") in addition to the journal, potion, and sack.

The real treasure in the mine lies above the pool of water behind the waterfall. Accessing the ledge behind the pool, either by jumping from a nearby ledge or using [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"), reveals a short passage ending in an alcove containing three gold ore veins. An unlootable skeleton, presumably Bern's, lies beneath a rock fall, revealing his likely fate. The skeleton clutches a pickaxe which may be taken.

## Notes

- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") may follow you to the tunnel with the ore veins, but will probably get stuck there unless you command them to stay and wait.
- Lost Prospect Mine also [appears](/wiki/Online:Lost_Prospect "Online:Lost Prospect") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- In the tunnel behind the waterfall, there is a blisterwort and an imp stool on your left that can't be harvested.

# Skyrim:Lost Relic

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dawnguard Dawnguard.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dawnguard_Dawnguard.png) | **Retrieve a relic of the original [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") |
| Location(s): | [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard"), [radiant dungeon](#Possible_Locations) |
| Reward: | [Dawnguard Rune Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Hammer "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Hammer"), [Dawnguard Rune Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Shield "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Shield"), [Dawnguard Rune Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Axe") |
| ID: | DLC1RH08 |

The Dawnguard Rune Axe, the Dawnguard Rune Hammer, and the Dawnguard Rune Shield

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius").
2. Retrieve the artifact requested.
3. Return to Florentius.

### The Lost Relics

*"I've been pouring*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *over some of the tomes left here in the keep."*

Speak to [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") after you have completed the first [Ancient Technology](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Technology "Skyrim:Ancient Technology") quest and a number of either [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar")'s or [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s side quests. Florentius, guided by the wishes of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay") as usual, will inform you: *"I've been pouring*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *over some of the tomes left here in the keep. Interesting stories, indeed. Seems the previous incarnation of the Dawnguard had, at one time, some interesting toys. Arkay and I think it could be a great advantage for us. You should look into retrieving it."* There are three parts to this quest, each appearing as a new quest of the same name in your journal. Florentius will recite what was written in the old tomes for each of the three artifacts:
**[Dawnguard Rune Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Hammer "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Hammer")**: *"A powerful warhammer imbued with magic that places warding runes on the ground to obliterate it's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *wielder's foes."*
**[Dawnguard Rune Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Shield "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Shield")**: *"A magical shield that when blocked with, surrounds it's*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *wielder with a holy aura that harms the undead."*
**[Dawnguard Rune Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Rune_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard Rune Axe")**: *"An axe imbued with magic fueled by the destruction of the unholy. With every victorious blow against an undead creature, its power grows."*

For each version of this quest you will be told to go to a random dungeon from the table below, where you'll find the artifact in the boss chest. When you return each artifact to Florentius, he will allow you to keep it: *"Well done! I said you'd return victorious, Arkay wasn't so sure. Wield it bravely."*
