Burning beehives at Goldenglow Estate

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Brynjolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Brynjolf "Skyrim:Brynjolf").
2. *(Optional)* Speak to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex").
3. *(Optional)* Enter using the sewer.
4. Proceed to [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate").
5. *(Optional)* Obtain the key to Aringoth's safe.
6. Burn three bee hives.
7. Open [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth")'s safe.
8. Retrieve the [Goldenglow Bill of Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Bill_of_Sale_(safe) "Skyrim:Goldenglow Bill of Sale (safe)").
9. Return to Brynjolf.

### Sweeter than Golden Honey

Once [Mercer](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey") has allowed you into the Guild, he'll challenge you with a new job. [Goldenglow Estate](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Estate "Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate") was once the Guild's sweetest deal. The Guild made sure that the honey flowed constantly to [Maven Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar")'s [meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery") by keeping the workforce in line and scaring off potential competitors. In return it was allowed to extort huge sums of money from [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth"), the owner. However, the shipments have suddenly ceased and when [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") was sent to investigate she found an army of mercenaries. Maven isn't pleased and it's your job to teach Aringoth a lesson by burning down three bee hives and clearing out his safe.

Before leaving, pay Vex a visit and she will tell you about a secret sewer entrance on the northwest side which will make it significantly easier to enter unseen.

### As Loud as an Angry Beehive...

Your first objective is to burn the beehives, which you can reach in two ways. The simplest route is to wade ashore on the northernmost island, dispatch the numerous mercenaries protecting the estate and then burn the hives. A stealthier solution is to wait until dusk, swim to the rocky outcrop to the west of the beehives and then clamber ashore, hidden by a small wooden wall.

The secret sewer entrance leading into the estate

To set the beehives on fire you can use a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), the [Fire Breath](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Breath "Skyrim:Fire Breath") Shout, or a [fire-based spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage#Spells "Skyrim:Fire Damage"); simply standing next to a hive with a torch or spell equipped will suffice. A rapid execution is important as three mercenaries will come rushing to investigate, so quickly burn the three southernmost beehives and then retreat behind the wall. Jump back into the lake and circle around to the northern island. Be careful not to burn more than three beehives, or you will forfeit your gold reward.

### ...and as Silent as a Skeever

Wade ashore underneath the wooden platform on the northwestern end of the island and dive into the sewer grate nearby. The sewer is only inhabited by a few [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever#Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), three of which can be taken out by using an oil slick and some fire. About half-way through is an adept-lock cell where you'll find the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")*. After leaving that room continue down the corridor and you will find a ladder back to the surface. Climb it and you will resurface next to the back entrance of the estate, which has an expert level lock and lands you in a more favorable location than the front door.

Alternatively, you can sneak your way to the front door, which is unlocked, or take out the mercenaries and enter through either door.

### Breaking and Entering

The Queen Bee Statue in Aringoth's quarters

Inside the estate you will find numerous mercenaries which you can either kill or sneak around. You should eventually arrive at a corridor patrolled by a mercenary while two more sit at a table. Avoid them by sneaking into the nearby dining room and you'll find yourself in front of a gate leading to the basement and a ladder leading to the second floor.

Heading upstairs will earn you more loot and you'll be able to take the safe's key off [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth"). The first mercenary can be avoided by slipping into a room on the left, traversing it and then moving down the corridor hugging the wall and using a wardrobe to screen you. In the last room, slowly sneak behind the back of a mercenary sitting at a table and pick open the door. Here you will find Aringoth and you can retrieve the safe key by either pickpocketing him, killing him or persuading him to hand it over. You must pass a hard-level [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to persuade Aringoth and, if you fail, he will attack you, alerting the nearby mercenary. There is also a [Queen Bee Statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Bee_Statue "Skyrim:Queen Bee Statue") on the nightstand next to the bed which can be sold to [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory").

### Sweep the Safe

The safe containing Aringoth's riches

Whether or not you have the key, unlock the metal gate once the mercenary patrolling the corridor has turned around and enter the basement. Sneak past or dispose of two mercenaries in the first room. Using a spell to set fire to the oil puddle leading up to his chair can aid you with dispatching the last mercenary. If you wish to remain undetected, sneak to the dark corner behind him, shoot an arrow down the corridor and slip away when he charges off to investigate. Alternatively, [invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Invisibility_(effect) "Skyrim:Invisibility (effect)") or the [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") [Throw Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Throw_Voice "Skyrim:Throw Voice") will also work.

Pick the safe or open it with its key and retrieve the [Goldenglow Bill of Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Bill_of_Sale_(safe) "Skyrim:Goldenglow Bill of Sale (safe)") and some gold. Before you leave, loot the nearby chest and scoop up some gold purses. A gate will lead you back into the sewers, so exit them and swim away to the shore.

### Reaping the Rewards

Head back to the guild and talk to Brynjolf. As long as you've completed the job to the letter, he'll be very pleased and reward you with a leveled amount of gold, as detailed below. If you burn more than three beehives, you will not get a reward, with Brynjolf saying, *"You've made a mess of things and Maven's furious. I told you not to burn more than three of the hives! I've smoothed things over with her for now, but you can forget your cut."* Either way, he'll also point you to Maven Black-Briar, who has requested you for a special job.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-5 | 50 |
| 6-10 | 100 |
| 11-15 | 200 |
| 16-20 | 300 |
| 21-26 | 400 |
| 27-31 | 500 |
| 32-36 | 600 |
| 37-41 | 700 |
| 42+ | 800 |

## Notes

- After speaking with Mercer, three [Thief Cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") barrels will appear around Riften.
- If [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has been completed, a leveled [Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") may attack the estate and mercenaries during the mission.

## Bugs

- When trying to burn the hives at Goldenglow Estate with a torch or a single-shot fire spell (like Firebolt and Fireball), the hive may not catch on fire the first time and may require that you hit it multiple times before it starts to burn. This may cause Brynjolf to act as if you had burned more than three hives, however, and result in you not getting paid even though you only burned three.
  - To avoid this, try using the Flames spell as it seems to work more effectively.
  - You can also alter Brynjolf's reaction by entering the following console command: `SetPapyrusQuestVar TG02 pTG02QuestFailure_var 0` before talking to him.

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15, 35.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TG02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TG02`.

Lund's Hut

**Lund's Hut** is a small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") northwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever").

## Related Quests

- **[When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Silver "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Silver"): Find a stash of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") armor.

### Exterior

To reach the building, take the road northwest out of Rorikstead and follow it until you come to a dirt path on the left leading to the shack. It is a single-level, fairly rundown building with a fenced-off porch area at the front. There are four skeevers using a couple moldy straw bales for bedding outside the building. Northwest of the shack a few paces is a cairn with a lit candle and a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring") (which may have fallen to the ground) on the edge and a basket containing three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on the ground. To the left of the building is a tree with two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") by the trunk. There are several [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") and more blue mountain flowers lining the path leading from the road to the shack.

### Lund's Hut

A skeever infestation

The building is unlocked and contains two more skeevers. The corpse of the original owner, [Lund](/wiki/Skyrim:Lund "Skyrim:Lund"), is in a single unusable bed in the eastern corner of this one-room structure. The place is a mess: [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), furniture, and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") are scattered around the room. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot at the foot of his bed (in Anniversary Edition this chest requires a key and cannot be picked; the key is obtained by completing the quest [When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") in a cast iron pot under the bed, and a [blue dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing") right in the corner between the bed and the wall, under the basket or caught in the spider web above the basket. Beside the bed, against the southeast wall is an end table with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on top. Along the rest of the southeast wall are a sack and barrel of foodstuffs, with a barrel of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") behind the first. In front of these is a low table with a mead barrel and two bottles of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead") on top. To the right of the barrels, against the southwest wall is a long wooden table, under which are two [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"). On the table are a bottle of [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), a bottle of alto wine, and several red apples.

To the right of the table are a wooden bench and a couple of chairs lying on their backs and various items of footwear and clothes underneath. To the right is a fireplace that is still lit, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and spit in front and a mounted skeever head above. On the mantelpiece is a [blue butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), and in front of the hearth are three wooden bowls; two contain pheasant breasts and the other contains a [chicken breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Chicken Breast"). In the western corner is another long wooden table and bench with a patch of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus growing beside it, and in the corner behind it are two more blue dartwings.

In the northern corner is an open crate containing a [butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing"), a sample of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), and various items of clothing, with a second butterfly wing between the crate and the wall. Along the northeast wall is a set of shelves with three common books, with more on the floor in front. Between the shelves and the entrance is another wooden bench, with a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") on top and a wall shelf above holding a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). Hanging from the ceiling above are a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid") and a bunch of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam").

## Bugs

- The door to Lund's Hut is owned by [Ulfberth War-Bear](/wiki/Skyrim:WhiterunUlfberthsHouseFaction "Skyrim:WhiterunUlfberthsHouseFaction").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- Although the exterior walls are made of wood, the interior is all stone.

# Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Farm: Lylvieve Family's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lylvieve+Family%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |

| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DragonBridgeFarm | |

| Location | |
| [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |

Lylvieve Family's House

**Lylvieve Family's House** is a small farmhouse on the northwestern side of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), located next to [Horgeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Horgeir's House").

It is home to [Azzada Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Azzada_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Azzada Lylvieve"), his wife [Michel](/wiki/Skyrim:Michel_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Michel Lylvieve"), and their children, [Julienne](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve") and [Clinton](/wiki/Skyrim:Clinton_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Clinton Lylvieve"). It consists of one zone, *[Lylvieve Family's House](#Lylvieve_Family.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Azzada Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Azzada_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Azzada Lylvieve")  [Clinton Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Clinton_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Clinton Lylvieve")  [Julienne Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve")  [Michel Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Michel_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Michel Lylvieve") |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

| Crops | Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 8 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  4 [Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") | 1 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg")  1 [Grain Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling")  1 [Wood Chopping Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") |

### Lylvieve Family's House

Ground floor

There are two levels to this home, including the ground floor and the basement. Upon entering, the right side holds a bedroom area, along the east wall. The double bed (belonging to the [Lylvieve Family House Occupants](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family_House_Occupants "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family House Occupants") faction) is flanked by a small table to the right and a non-respawning dresser to the left. Atop the table are five loose gold coins and a basket containing four [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"). The dresser holds a [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") (filled), two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), two [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), a [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), and a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina"). Along the north wall is a set of shelves holding four bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and one bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") on the top shelf, along with three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), three [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), and two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on the middle shelf. On the floor to the right of these shelves is a woven basket containing three [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). Above the shelves are some hanging ingredients, including two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, one dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and two portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). At the center of the room is a large dining table which holds a messy arrangement of food, including two [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), one [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), three loaves of bread, two chicken's eggs, two bottles of alto wine, and two pieces of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"). In the southwest corner of the room, there are two respawning meat barrels.

Basement

Proceeding down the stairs to the basement, the children's bedroom area is along the east wall, while the rest of the room is used for general storage. A child's bed owned by [Clinton](/wiki/Skyrim:Clinton_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Clinton Lylvieve") is in the northeast corner, while a single bed owned by [Julienne](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve") is in the southeast corner. At the foot of each bed is a small non-respawning chest. Along the north wall, there is a small round table holding one goat cheese wedge, one loaf of bread, and two boiled creme treats. To the left of the table is a respawning food barrel, and between them are four freshly caught [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging above. Another respawning food barrel can be found below the stairs, among various clutter.

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_House_Key "Skyrim:Lylvieve House Key") to which is carried by all four members of the Lylvieve family.
- A [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling") can be found behind the house, which can be used to produce [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") from [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.

# Skyrim:Magic Student

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Secunda](/wiki/User:Secunda "User:Secunda"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **A [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Student "Skyrim:Student") wants your help with his training.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | A few [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") |
| ID: | WIChangeLocation04 |

The Student utilizing his flames spell

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Encounter the [aspiring wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Student "Skyrim:Student").
2. Help him perfect his spell technique.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When entering any of the major cities, you may come across a [wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Student "Skyrim:Student") who claims to want to join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)"). He will then ask that you teach him a few [spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Spells "Skyrim:Spells"), usually [ward spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward#Spells "Skyrim:Ward"):

:   *"I've finally found you! I want to join the College of Winterhold. But I need help with my wards. Can you teach me?"*
:   **Sure, I can teach you.**
:   *"Really? Great! Okay. So, first, you raise your ward and I'll throw a little spell at it. That way I can see the 'right' way to do things."*

He will cast his spell and then ask you to cast yours:

:   *"Get your ward ready."*
:   *"Great! Now I'm going to cast some spells at you. Keep your ward up so I can study it."*

As he casts a spell against your ward, usually Flames:

:   *"I think I see what I was doing wrong... All right. That should do it. I think I'm ready to try the College again. Thanks!"*

He will then reward you with a small number of [scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls").

## Notes

- If you have a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), tell them to wait a short distance away. If you don't, they will attack the wizard when he attacks you.

## Bugs

- Loading through doors (into your house for example) will result in the Student disappearing from the city when you go back outside. A quest marker will be present, but is not visible on the map, leaving no way to finish or remove the quest from the log.

## Quest Stages

| Magic Student (WIChangeLocation04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Use Ward while Student attacks you. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 110, 200, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIChangeLocation04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIChangeLocation04`.

# Skyrim:Main Quest

## Overview

Skyrim's **main quest** consists of seventeen required quests and two optional quests. During these quests you discover your heritage as the [Dovahkiin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin"), learn why [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") have returned to the world, and find a way to respond to the dragon threat. Completing the main quest will take approximately 15-30 hours depending on your character's level. Eight [achievements](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") (170 points; 7 Bronze and 1 Gold) are directly tied to completing the main quest; in addition, several [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts#Achievements "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts")-related achievements are inevitably unlocked during the quests. Quests belonging to the main quest are marked in your journal by the dragon head knotwork, which is pictured above.

1. **[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")**: Escape [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") custody and a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") attack. ( 10 pts/Bronze)
2. **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
3. **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(quest) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (quest)")**: Retrieve the [Dragonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonstone "Skyrim:Dragonstone"). ( 10 pts/Bronze)
4. **[Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising")**: Investigate a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") sighting near [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
5. **[The Way of the Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Way_of_the_Voice "Skyrim:The Way of the Voice")**: Meet the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"). ( 20 pts/Bronze)
6. **[The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Horn_of_Jurgen_Windcaller "Skyrim:The Horn of Jurgen Windcaller")**: Retrieve a [Greybeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") artifact from [Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav").
7. **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
8. **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"). ( 20 pts/Bronze)
9. **[A Cornered Rat](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Cornered_Rat "Skyrim:A Cornered Rat")**: Locate [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern").
10. **[Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall")**: Locate the prophecy within [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"). ( 20 pts/Bronze)
11. **[The Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World")**: Receive a lesson from [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
12. **[Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge")**: Recover an [Elder Scroll](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Scroll "Skyrim:Elder Scroll") to learn an [Ancient Secret](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend"). ( 20 pts/Bronze)
13. **[Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane")**: Exploit the Time-Wound to learn [Dragonrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonrend "Skyrim:Dragonrend") and defeat [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") at the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World").
14. **[The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen")**: Capture and interrogate [an ally](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") of [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"). ( 20 pts/Bronze)
    - (optional) **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").
    - (optional) **[Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(quest) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)")**: Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
15. **[The World-Eater's Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:The_World-Eater%27s_Eyrie "Skyrim:The World-Eater's Eyrie")**: Battle through [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn") to reach [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")'s portal to [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").
16. **[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)")**: Seek out [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") within [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").
17. **[Dragonslayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer "Skyrim:Dragonslayer")**: Put an end to the [World-Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin"). ( 50 pts/Gold)

# Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. |  |  |

| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | Progress towards becoming [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") |
| ID: | FavorJarlsMakeFriends |

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive in any of the nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") of Skyrim. The name of the objective appearing in your journal will be one of the following, depending upon the hold:

- Assist the people of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch")
- Assist the people of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")
- Assist the people of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")
- Assist the people of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")
- Assist the people of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")
- Assist the people of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach")
- Assist the people of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift") (see [notes](#Notes))
- Assist the people of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Thane of Whiterun")
- Assist the people of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold")

## Quick Walkthrough

Before starting this quest, you must first befriend the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the hold.

1. Speak to the jarl to receive the quest.
2. Improve the [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") of three or five people of that hold, usually by doing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them.
3. Return to the jarl.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will need to improve the disposition of three people for the minor holds Falkreath, Hjaalmarch, the Pale, and Winterhold. For the major holds Eastmarch, Haafingar, the Reach, the Rift, and Whiterun, you will need to help five people. The people you help must be ordinary citizens of the hold; members of [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") and Orcs living in [strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") do not count, and neither does befriending the hold's [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") (as that is a prerequisite to being given the objective).

Disposition can be improved in any of the following ways:

- by performing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") on their behalf
- by completing certain [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")
- investing 500 gold in stores, if you have the [investor perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor")
- dropping some armor pieces in front of citizens and [allowing them to keep it](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Reactions "Skyrim:World Interactions")
- [rescuing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") kidnapped citizens

Citizens that you befriend before starting this quest also count towards your total, and as such, it is possible to complete this objective for a particular hold immediately after starting the Thane quest. Also, citizens that you befriended which then died still count towards your total. (Usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for this quest.

## Notes

- While [the Rift thane quest](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") is active, most of its objectives do not show up in your journal. The Rift thane quest uses its own code to replace the functions of this quest, so Objective 20 is never assigned. The requirement to assist citizens of the Rift is replaced by an invisible requirement to complete [miscellaneous objectives in Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften#Miscellaneous "Skyrim:Riften"), which starts automatically after completing [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"). The game will track the number of Riften quests you complete, unlike in other holds where you are required to ask the jarl if there is something you can do to help first. Once you have completed enough miscellaneous quests, you will be given an objective to return to the Jarl of Riften.
- If Balgruuf is Jarl of Whiterun, you cannot receive this quest from him. He will make you Thane as a quest reward for completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), which is early in the main quest. Only if you side with the Stormcloaks and remove him from power is this quest available in Whiterun.

## Bugs

- "Assist the people of Haafingar" may not be cleared from your quest log by Solitude's jarl once completed, though you are able to become a thane and gain a housecarl in your home (once purchased). The concern may be complicated by having already helped five people before talking to the jarl for the first time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering the console command `setobjectivecompleted FavorJarlsMakeFriends 30 1` after becoming a thane may resolve this.
  - Continuing to assist the people of Haafingar can cause the counter to update to 6/5, at which point the objective is completed and cleared from the quest log.

## Quest Stages

| Making Friends and Influencing People (FavorJarlsMakeFriends) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Assist the people of the Reach (<Global=FriendsCountReach>/5) |
| 15 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Reach)* |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Assist the people of the Rift (<Global=FriendsCountRift>/5) |
| 25 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Rift)* |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Assist the people of Haafingar (<Global=FriendsCountHaafingar>/5) |
| 35 |  | *(Quest Completed for Haafingar)* |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Assist the people of Whiterun (<Global=FriendsCountWhiterun>/5) |
| 45 |  | *(Quest Completed for Whiterun)* |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Assist the people of Eastmarch (<Global=FriendsCountEastmarch>/5) |
| 55 |  | *(Quest Completed for Eastmarch)* |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Assist the people of Hjaalmarch (<Global=FriendsCountHjaalmarch>/3) |
| 65 |  | *(Quest Completed for Hjaalmarch)* |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Assist the people of the Pale (<Global=FriendsCountPale>/3) |
| 75 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Pale)* |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Assist the people of Winterhold (<Global=FriendsCountWinterhold>/3) |
| 85 |  | *(Quest Completed for Winterhold)* |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Assist the people of Falkreath (<Global=FriendsCountFalkreath>/3) |
| 95 |  | *(Quest Completed for Falkreath)* |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FavorJarlsMakeFriends stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FavorJarlsMakeFriends`.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. ## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive in any of the nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") of Skyrim. The name of the objective appearing in your journal will be one of the following, depending upon the hold:

- Assist the people of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch")
- Assist the people of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")
- Assist the people of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")
- Assist the people of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")
- Assist the people of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")
- Assist the people of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach")
- Assist the people of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift") (see [notes](#Notes))
- Assist the people of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Thane of Whiterun")
- Assist the people of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold")

## Quick Walkthrough

Before starting this quest, you must first befriend the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the hold.

1. Speak to the jarl to receive the quest.
2. Improve the [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") of three or five people of that hold, usually by doing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them.
3. Return to the jarl.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will need to improve the disposition of three people for the minor holds Falkreath, Hjaalmarch, the Pale, and Winterhold. For the major holds Eastmarch, Haafingar, the Reach, the Rift, and Whiterun, you will need to help five people. The people you help must be ordinary citizens of the hold; members of [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") and Orcs living in [strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") do not count, and neither does befriending the hold's [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") (as that is a prerequisite to being given the objective).

Disposition can be improved in any of the following ways:

- by performing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") on their behalf
- by completing certain [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")
- investing 500 gold in stores, if you have the [investor perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor")
- dropping some armor pieces in front of citizens and [allowing them to keep it](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Reactions "Skyrim:World Interactions")
- [rescuing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") kidnapped citizens

Citizens that you befriend before starting this quest also count towards your total, and as such, it is possible to complete this objective for a particular hold immediately after starting the Thane quest. Also, citizens that you befriended which then died still count towards your total. (Usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for this quest.

## Notes

- While [the Rift thane quest](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") is active, most of its objectives do not show up in your journal. The Rift thane quest uses its own code to replace the functions of this quest, so Objective 20 is never assigned. The requirement to assist citizens of the Rift is replaced by an invisible requirement to complete [miscellaneous objectives in Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften#Miscellaneous "Skyrim:Riften"), which starts automatically after completing [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"). He will make you Thane as a quest reward for completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), which is early in the main quest. Only if you side with the Stormcloaks and remove him from power is this quest available in Whiterun.

## Bugs

- "Assist the people of Haafingar" may not be cleared from your quest log by Solitude's jarl once completed, though you are able to become a thane and gain a housecarl in your home (once purchased). The concern may be complicated by having already helped five people before talking to the jarl for the first time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering the console command `setobjectivecompleted FavorJarlsMakeFriends 30 1` after becoming a thane may resolve this.
  - Continuing to assist the people of Haafingar can cause the counter to update to 6/5, at which point the objective is completed and cleared from the quest log.

## Overview

| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Assist the people of Winterhold (<Global=FriendsCountWinterhold>/3) |
| 85 |  | *(Quest Completed for Winterhold)* |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Assist the people of Falkreath (<Global=FriendsCountFalkreath>/3) |
| 95 |  | *(Quest Completed for Falkreath)* |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FavorJarlsMakeFriends stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FavorJarlsMakeFriends`.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |
| --- |
| **This article could benefit from an image**. See [Help:Images](/wiki/Help:Images "Help:Images") for information on how to upload images. Please remove this template from the page when finished. |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Assist the people of the hold.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | Progress towards becoming [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") |
| ID: | FavorJarlsMakeFriends |

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive in any of the nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") of Skyrim. The name of the objective appearing in your journal will be one of the following, depending upon the hold:

- Assist the people of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch")
- Assist the people of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")
- Assist the people of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")
- Assist the people of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")
- Assist the people of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")
- Assist the people of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach")
- Assist the people of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift") (see [notes](#Notes))
- Assist the people of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Thane of Whiterun")
- Assist the people of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold")

## Quick Walkthrough

Before starting this quest, you must first befriend the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the hold.

1. Speak to the jarl to receive the quest.
2. Improve the [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") of three or five people of that hold, usually by doing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them.
3. Return to the jarl.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will need to improve the disposition of three people for the minor holds Falkreath, Hjaalmarch, the Pale, and Winterhold. For the major holds Eastmarch, Haafingar, the Reach, the Rift, and Whiterun, you will need to help five people. The people you help must be ordinary citizens of the hold; members of [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") and Orcs living in [strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") do not count, and neither does befriending the hold's [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") (as that is a prerequisite to being given the objective).

Disposition can be improved in any of the following ways:

- by performing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") on their behalf
- by completing certain [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")
- investing 500 gold in stores, if you have the [investor perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor")
- dropping some armor pieces in front of citizens and [allowing them to keep it](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Reactions "Skyrim:World Interactions")
- [rescuing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") kidnapped citizens

Citizens that you befriend before starting this quest also count towards your total, and as such, it is possible to complete this objective for a particular hold immediately after starting the Thane quest. Also, citizens that you befriended which then died still count towards your total. (Usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for this quest.

## Notes

- While [the Rift thane quest](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") is active, most of its objectives do not show up in your journal. The Rift thane quest uses its own code to replace the functions of this quest, so Objective 20 is never assigned. The requirement to assist citizens of the Rift is replaced by an invisible requirement to complete [miscellaneous objectives in Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften#Miscellaneous "Skyrim:Riften"), which starts automatically after completing [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"). The game will track the number of Riften quests you complete, unlike in other holds where you are required to ask the jarl if there is something you can do to help first. Once you have completed enough miscellaneous quests, you will be given an objective to return to the Jarl of Riften.
- If Balgruuf is Jarl of Whiterun, you cannot receive this quest from him. He will make you Thane as a quest reward for completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), which is early in the main quest. Only if you side with the Stormcloaks and remove him from power is this quest available in Whiterun.

## Bugs

- "Assist the people of Haafingar" may not be cleared from your quest log by Solitude's jarl once completed, though you are able to become a thane and gain a housecarl in your home (once purchased). The concern may be complicated by having already helped five people before talking to the jarl for the first time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering the console command `setobjectivecompleted FavorJarlsMakeFriends 30 1` after becoming a thane may resolve this.
  - Continuing to assist the people of Haafingar can cause the counter to update to 6/5, at which point the objective is completed and cleared from the quest log.

## Quest Stages

| Making Friends and Influencing People (FavorJarlsMakeFriends) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Assist the people of the Reach (<Global=FriendsCountReach>/5) |
| 15 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Reach)* |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Assist the people of the Rift (<Global=FriendsCountRift>/5) |
| 25 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Rift)* |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Assist the people of Haafingar (<Global=FriendsCountHaafingar>/5) |
| 35 |  | *(Quest Completed for Haafingar)* |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Assist the people of Whiterun (<Global=FriendsCountWhiterun>/5) |
| 45 |  | *(Quest Completed for Whiterun)* |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Assist the people of Eastmarch (<Global=FriendsCountEastmarch>/5) |
| 55 |  | *(Quest Completed for Eastmarch)* |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Assist the people of Hjaalmarch (<Global=FriendsCountHjaalmarch>/3) |
| 65 |  | *(Quest Completed for Hjaalmarch)* |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Assist the people of the Pale (<Global=FriendsCountPale>/3) |
| 75 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Pale)* |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Assist the people of Winterhold (<Global=FriendsCountWinterhold>/3) |
| 85 |  | *(Quest Completed for Winterhold)* |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Assist the people of Falkreath (<Global=FriendsCountFalkreath>/3) |
| 95 |  | *(Quest Completed for Falkreath)* |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FavorJarlsMakeFriends stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FavorJarlsMakeFriends`.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. - by completing certain [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")
- investing 500 gold in stores, if you have the [investor perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor")
- dropping some armor pieces in front of citizens and [allowing them to keep it](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Reactions "Skyrim:World Interactions")
- [rescuing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") kidnapped citizens

Citizens that you befriend before starting this quest also count towards your total, and as such, it is possible to complete this objective for a particular hold immediately after starting the Thane quest. Also, citizens that you befriended which then died still count towards your total. (Usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for this quest.

## Notes

- While [the Rift thane quest](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") is active, most of its objectives do not show up in your journal. The Rift thane quest uses its own code to replace the functions of this quest, so Objective 20 is never assigned. The requirement to assist citizens of the Rift is replaced by an invisible requirement to complete [miscellaneous objectives in Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften#Miscellaneous "Skyrim:Riften"), which starts automatically after completing [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"). The game will track the number of Riften quests you complete, unlike in other holds where you are required to ask the jarl if there is something you can do to help first. Once you have completed enough miscellaneous quests, you will be given an objective to return to the Jarl of Riften.
- If Balgruuf is Jarl of Whiterun, you cannot receive this quest from him. He will make you Thane as a quest reward for completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), which is early in the main quest. Only if you side with the Stormcloaks and remove him from power is this quest available in Whiterun.

## Bugs

- "Assist the people of Haafingar" may not be cleared from your quest log by Solitude's jarl once completed, though you are able to become a thane and gain a housecarl in your home (once purchased). The concern may be complicated by having already helped five people before talking to the jarl for the first time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering the console command `setobjectivecompleted FavorJarlsMakeFriends 30 1` after becoming a thane may resolve this.
  - Continuing to assist the people of Haafingar can cause the counter to update to 6/5, at which point the objective is completed and cleared from the quest log.

## Quest Stages

| Making Friends and Influencing People (FavorJarlsMakeFriends) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Assist the people of the Reach (<Global=FriendsCountReach>/5) |
| 15 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Reach)* |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Assist the people of the Rift (<Global=FriendsCountRift>/5) |
| 25 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Rift)* |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Assist the people of Haafingar (<Global=FriendsCountHaafingar>/5) |
| 35 |  | *(Quest Completed for Haafingar)* |

| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Assist the people of the Pale (<Global=FriendsCountPale>/3) |
| 75 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Pale)* |

| 85 |  | *(Quest Completed for Winterhold)* |

| 95 |  | *(Quest Completed for Falkreath)* |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FavorJarlsMakeFriends stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FavorJarlsMakeFriends`.

# Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by multiple users, *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Nephele](/wiki/User:Nephele "User:Nephele"), checked by [RobinHood70](/wiki/User:RobinHood70 "User:RobinHood70") |

|  |
| --- |
| **This article could benefit from an image**. See [Help:Images](/wiki/Help:Images "Help:Images") for information on how to upload images. Please remove this template from the page when finished. |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Assist the people of the hold.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | Progress towards becoming [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") |
| ID: | FavorJarlsMakeFriends |

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive in any of the nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") of Skyrim. The name of the objective appearing in your journal will be one of the following, depending upon the hold:

- Assist the people of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch")
- Assist the people of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")
- Assist the people of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")
- Assist the people of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")
- Assist the people of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")
- Assist the people of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach")
- Assist the people of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift") (see [notes](#Notes))
- Assist the people of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Thane of Whiterun")
- Assist the people of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold")

## Quick Walkthrough

Before starting this quest, you must first befriend the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the hold.

1. Speak to the jarl to receive the quest.
2. Improve the [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") of three or five people of that hold, usually by doing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them.
3. Return to the jarl.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will need to improve the disposition of three people for the minor holds Falkreath, Hjaalmarch, the Pale, and Winterhold. For the major holds Eastmarch, Haafingar, the Reach, the Rift, and Whiterun, you will need to help five people. The people you help must be ordinary citizens of the hold; members of [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") and Orcs living in [strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") do not count, and neither does befriending the hold's [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") (as that is a prerequisite to being given the objective).

Disposition can be improved in any of the following ways:

- by performing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") on their behalf
- by completing certain [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")
- investing 500 gold in stores, if you have the [investor perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor")
- dropping some armor pieces in front of citizens and [allowing them to keep it](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Reactions "Skyrim:World Interactions")
- [rescuing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") kidnapped citizens

Citizens that you befriend before starting this quest also count towards your total, and as such, it is possible to complete this objective for a particular hold immediately after starting the Thane quest. Also, citizens that you befriended which then died still count towards your total. (Usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for this quest.

## Notes

- While [the Rift thane quest](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") is active, most of its objectives do not show up in your journal. The Rift thane quest uses its own code to replace the functions of this quest, so Objective 20 is never assigned. The requirement to assist citizens of the Rift is replaced by an invisible requirement to complete [miscellaneous objectives in Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften#Miscellaneous "Skyrim:Riften"), which starts automatically after completing [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"). The game will track the number of Riften quests you complete, unlike in other holds where you are required to ask the jarl if there is something you can do to help first. Once you have completed enough miscellaneous quests, you will be given an objective to return to the Jarl of Riften.
- If Balgruuf is Jarl of Whiterun, you cannot receive this quest from him. He will make you Thane as a quest reward for completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), which is early in the main quest. Only if you side with the Stormcloaks and remove him from power is this quest available in Whiterun.

## Bugs

- "Assist the people of Haafingar" may not be cleared from your quest log by Solitude's jarl once completed, though you are able to become a thane and gain a housecarl in your home (once purchased). The concern may be complicated by having already helped five people before talking to the jarl for the first time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering the console command `setobjectivecompleted FavorJarlsMakeFriends 30 1` after becoming a thane may resolve this.
  - Continuing to assist the people of Haafingar can cause the counter to update to 6/5, at which point the objective is completed and cleared from the quest log.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FavorJarlsMakeFriends stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FavorJarlsMakeFriends`.

# Skyrim:Making Friends and Influencing People

## Overview

| **Assist the people of the hold.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | Progress towards becoming [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") |
| ID: | FavorJarlsMakeFriends |

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive in any of the nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") of Skyrim. The name of the objective appearing in your journal will be one of the following, depending upon the hold:

- Assist the people of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch")
- Assist the people of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")
- Assist the people of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")
- Assist the people of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")
- Assist the people of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")
- Assist the people of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach")
- Assist the people of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift") (see [notes](#Notes))
- Assist the people of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Thane of Whiterun")
- Assist the people of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold")

## Quick Walkthrough

Before starting this quest, you must first befriend the [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of the hold.

1. Speak to the jarl to receive the quest.
2. Improve the [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") of three or five people of that hold, usually by doing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them.
3. Return to the jarl.

## Detailed Walkthrough

You will need to improve the disposition of three people for the minor holds Falkreath, Hjaalmarch, the Pale, and Winterhold. For the major holds Eastmarch, Haafingar, the Reach, the Rift, and Whiterun, you will need to help five people. The people you help must be ordinary citizens of the hold; members of [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders") and Orcs living in [strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") do not count, and neither does befriending the hold's [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") (as that is a prerequisite to being given the objective).

Disposition can be improved in any of the following ways:

- by performing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") on their behalf
- by completing certain [side quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Side_Quests "Skyrim:Side Quests")
- investing 500 gold in stores, if you have the [investor perk](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor")
- dropping some armor pieces in front of citizens and [allowing them to keep it](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Reactions "Skyrim:World Interactions")
- [rescuing](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_Mission "Skyrim:Rescue Mission") kidnapped citizens

Citizens that you befriend before starting this quest also count towards your total, and as such, it is possible to complete this objective for a particular hold immediately after starting the Thane quest. Also, citizens that you befriended which then died still count towards your total. (Usually in those cases, you will have received an [Inheritance](/wiki/Skyrim:Inheritance "Skyrim:Inheritance").) Note that if you befriend the same citizen twice, it only counts once for this quest.

## Notes

- While [the Rift thane quest](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!") is active, most of its objectives do not show up in your journal. The Rift thane quest uses its own code to replace the functions of this quest, so Objective 20 is never assigned. The requirement to assist citizens of the Rift is replaced by an invisible requirement to complete [miscellaneous objectives in Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften#Miscellaneous "Skyrim:Riften"), which starts automatically after completing [Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand"). The game will track the number of Riften quests you complete, unlike in other holds where you are required to ask the jarl if there is something you can do to help first. Once you have completed enough miscellaneous quests, you will be given an objective to return to the Jarl of Riften.
- If Balgruuf is Jarl of Whiterun, you cannot receive this quest from him. He will make you Thane as a quest reward for completing [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), which is early in the main quest. Only if you side with the Stormcloaks and remove him from power is this quest available in Whiterun.

## Bugs

- "Assist the people of Haafingar" may not be cleared from your quest log by Solitude's jarl once completed, though you are able to become a thane and gain a housecarl in your home (once purchased). The concern may be complicated by having already helped five people before talking to the jarl for the first time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.
  -  Entering the console command `setobjectivecompleted FavorJarlsMakeFriends 30 1` after becoming a thane may resolve this.
  - Continuing to assist the people of Haafingar can cause the counter to update to 6/5, at which point the objective is completed and cleared from the quest log.

## Quest Stages

| Making Friends and Influencing People (FavorJarlsMakeFriends) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Assist the people of the Reach (<Global=FriendsCountReach>/5) |
| 15 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Reach)* |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Assist the people of the Rift (<Global=FriendsCountRift>/5) |
| 25 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Rift)* |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Assist the people of Haafingar (<Global=FriendsCountHaafingar>/5) |
| 35 |  | *(Quest Completed for Haafingar)* |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Assist the people of Whiterun (<Global=FriendsCountWhiterun>/5) |
| 45 |  | *(Quest Completed for Whiterun)* |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Assist the people of Eastmarch (<Global=FriendsCountEastmarch>/5) |
| 55 |  | *(Quest Completed for Eastmarch)* |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Assist the people of Hjaalmarch (<Global=FriendsCountHjaalmarch>/3) |
| 65 |  | *(Quest Completed for Hjaalmarch)* |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Assist the people of the Pale (<Global=FriendsCountPale>/3) |
| 75 |  | *(Quest Completed for the Pale)* |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Assist the people of Winterhold (<Global=FriendsCountWinterhold>/3) |
| 85 |  | *(Quest Completed for Winterhold)* |
| 90 |  | *Objective 90:* Assist the people of Falkreath (<Global=FriendsCountFalkreath>/3) |
| 95 |  | *(Quest Completed for Falkreath)* |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FavorJarlsMakeFriends stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FavorJarlsMakeFriends`.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Making_Friends_and_Influencing_People&action=edit).*

## Overview

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive in any of the nine [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") of Skyrim. The name of the objective appearing in your journal will be one of the following, depending upon the hold:

- Assist the people of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch")
- Assist the people of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Falkreath "Skyrim:Thane of Falkreath")
- Assist the people of [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar")
- Assist the people of [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Hjaalmarch")
- Assist the people of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")
- Assist the people of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:Thane of the Reach")
- Assist the people of [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Rift "Skyrim:Thane of the Rift") (see [notes](#Notes))
- Assist the people of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Whiterun "Skyrim:Thane of Whiterun")
- Assist the people of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold")

1. Speak to the jarl to receive the quest.
2. Improve the [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") of three or five people of that hold, usually by doing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") for them.
3. Return to the jarl.

- by performing [favor quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors") on their behalf
