# Skyrim:Mara's Eye Den

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Mara's Eye Den ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mara%27s+Eye+Den)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MarasEyePond01 | |
| Region | |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | |
| Location | |
| Southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") North of [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill") | |

Mara's Eye Den

**Mara's Eye Den** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). It contains only one zone, *[Mara's Eye Den](#Mara.27s_Eye_Den)*.

The cave, on the central island of [Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond"), was once an underground smuggling hideout before its current occupation by two vampires.

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Information on the exterior can be found at [Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond").

### Mara's Eye Den

Storage area

Flooded area

Upon entering, you are at the end of a short tunnel that opens in front of you into a small cave. Two rock pillars support the ceiling, and many crates, barrels, and sacks are scattered around the cave. You are at the top of the cave, with wooden planking and a ramp descending to a flooded area at the bottom. On your right are several crates, barrels, sacks, and an apprentice-locked chest along the wall and stacked next to a statue. On the statue is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), which can be difficult to pick up.

Around the first pillar are more crates, barrels, and sacks, and on top of one of the crates is a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potions"). Around the far side of the same pillar is an open crate containing two copies of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* and copies of *[A Minor Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Minor_Maze "Skyrim:A Minor Maze")*, *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")*, *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*, and the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")*. There is also a filled [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"). Between the two pillars are two barrels and an open crate containing a lootable skeleton. There is another barrel by the second pillar, and just around the corner is a slightly raised area with two single beds on which the two vampires may be sleeping. Between the beds is an end table holding a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Poisons "Skyrim:Potions") and a copy of *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*, and leaning against one of the beds is a random one-handed weapon, which may be [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

Smuggler's journal

Against the south wall is a small wooden table with two chairs. The table holds a medium coin purse, an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), a [sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(item) "Skyrim:Sapphire (item)"), four loose [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins, a [gold necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Necklace"), a [gold ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Ring"), and a [smuggler's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Smuggler%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Smuggler's Journal") which describes what took place in this small subterranean sanctuary. Around the cave are several empty body-shaped boxes, which are probably part of the shipment mentioned in the journal. Several of the barrels contain ingredients. To the southwest against the wall is a campfire with the dead [smuggler](/wiki/Skyrim:Smuggler "Skyrim:Smuggler") lying next to it. An executioner's block, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), and a couple of gory skulls are to the right of the fire, and a long table and a pair of benches with gory human remains are nearby. The vampires can also occasionally be found here, with one of them feasting and the other playing a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum").

Following the ramp down to the flooded area, there is an unlocked boss chest on your right, and two large cages are in front of you. The first is level-locked, and may be empty, or may contain a corpse related to a radiant quest targeting this cave; the second is unlocked and contains the body of a dead [Vigilant of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr").

# Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond

## Overview

Mara's Eye Pond

**Mara's Eye Pond** is a small lake due east of [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock").

There is an island in the center of the lake that hides a trapdoor, which is the entrance to [Mara's Eye Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Den "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Den"), a [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") inhabited by leveled [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). Quests pointing to this location will lead you down into the cave under the lake.

[Gallows Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Hall_(place) "Skyrim:Gallows Hall (place)") is on the northern side of the pond.

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dreams of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Dreams_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Dreams of the Dead")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Hall "Skyrim:Gallows Hall"): Unlock the secrets of a necromancer's lair and make it your own.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Mara's Pond

There are two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") near the shore, to the north, south, and west-southwest respectively. A [clay](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay") deposit([HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")) can be found by the edge of the water to the west. Several [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") call this home, both around the shore and on the island in the middle. Strangely there are no plants that can be harvested growing along the shoreline around the lake. To the east is a cart containing a crate (and a bottle of skooma), with a second crate on the ground next to it. On the island there is a large rotten tree stump with a [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus growing on it and inside it there is the trapdoor entrance to [Mara's Eye Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Den "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Den"). There is a small rowboat pulled up on the island shore, with a crate, a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack, and an oar onboard.

## Notes

- With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") Creation, Mara's Eye Pond is a reliable source of [goldfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldfish "Skyrim:Goldfish") for [Catch of the Day](/wiki/Skyrim:Catch_of_the_Day "Skyrim:Catch of the Day") and [Bounty: Goldfish!](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Goldfish! "Skyrim:Bounty: Goldfish!") as a walk through the waters can net you between 3-6 of the flaxen fish.
- The pond gets its name from the way it looks from above. The pond is the shape of an eye and the small island in the middle, Mara's Eye, resembles a pupil.
- This location is only marked as cleared once you also clear Mara's Eye Den.

# Skyrim:March of the Dead

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Stop the [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") attacks on [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") |
| Location(s): | [Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm"),  [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth") |
| Reward: | [Champion's Cudgel](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Cudgel "Skyrim:Champion's Cudgel"), Leveled gold |
| ID: | DLC2RR01 |
| Suggested Level: | 20 |

Who is in charge of [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth")?

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Kill the [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") attacking [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") at [Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm").
2. Speak to Captain Veleth.
3. Search the Attius Farm for clues, and give the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Declaration_of_War "Skyrim:Declaration of War") you find to Captain Veleth.
4. Kill [General Falx Carius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Falx_Carius "Skyrim:General Falx Carius") at [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth").
5. Return to Captain Veleth.

### Aiding the Captain

Captain Veleth fights the ash spawn

[Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") is the leader of the [Redoran Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), the capital of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), his powers only surpassed by [Councilor Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn") and his second-in-command [Adril Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Adril_Arano "Skyrim:Adril Arano"). Recently, Raven Rock has experienced several attacks by [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") and Captain Veleth is naturally trying to figure out what is going on. South of Raven Rock lies the burned-out [Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm") where you will find Captain Veleth fighting several ash spawn, immediately starting the quest. Help him defeat the enemies and he will be quite grateful, saying: *"Thanks... I wasn't sure I'd make it off this farm alive. I wish I could have said the same for my man here."*, obviously referring to the dead [Redoran Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard_(dead) "Skyrim:Redoran Guard (dead)") nearby. He then proceeds to tell you about the ash spawn attacks and that he was searching for clues at the old farm when he was attacked. You will now have three different options, each with a different response:

**I'd be glad to lend you a hand.** *"Good, I can use all the help I can get."*
**I could lend you a hand... for a price.** *"Hmm. I think I could talk the councilor into paying you, and I could use an extra pair of hands."*
**Seems like a waste of time to me.** *"It's easy to criticize when you're just a visitor here. Since you're brimming with self-confidence, maybe you'd care to take over for me?"*

### Declaration of War

Regardless of your choice, Captain Veleth will then proceed to tell you why he was at the farm and task you: *"We were searching the farm when the ash spawn ambushed us. Have a look around and see if you can turn up anything useful."* You can now ask him several questions about the attacks and he will explain that he believes that someone is controlling the ash spawn and that the abandoned farm is his only clue as the enemies seem to emerge from there. Search the ash piles from the defeated enemies and you will find the *[Declaration of War](/wiki/Skyrim:Declaration_of_War "Skyrim:Declaration of War")*, a strange note written by [Falx Carius](/wiki/Lore:Falx_Carius "Lore:Falx Carius"), a general living at [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth"). Tell Captain Veleth about the letter and he will be surprised and tell you about the author of the note: *"Carius was the Imperial garrison commander at Fort Frostmoth, but he died over 200 years ago when the [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") leveled the place. There's no way he could still be alive."* He will then ask you to investigate while he "rallies the guard" back in Raven Rock.

### Fort Frostmoth

While Captain Veleth returns to Raven Rock, head east from the farm and you will soon arrive at the ash-covered [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth"), where a mysterious voice will shout out: *"Men, an invader has entered the fort! Prepare yourselves for an ambush!"* After this, several ash spawn will attack and shower you with firebolt spells while the voice continues: *"Fort Frostmoth will never fall! Long live the Empire!"* Fight them all and enter the fort. The interior is covered in ashes and old imperial armor sits on the knocked-over shelves, hinting at the original inhabitants 200 years back. Before long more ash spawn will detect you and attack, so pick the fight and locate the path to the north. In the next chamber, search around for the skeletal remains of [Maximian Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Maximian_Axius "Skyrim:Maximian Axius") and read all of [his letters](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Letter_to_Selina_I "Skyrim:A Letter to Selina I") to Selina for a bit of background story of what happened at the fort when Red Mountain erupted. The path to the west leads to a dead end and a nest of [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider"). A gate with a master lock gains access to a storeroom with all the ingredients needed to make a large quantity of Elsweyr Fondue.

### Falx Carius

*"Fort Frostmoth will never fall! Long live the Empire!"*

Take the northern path and you will end up in a huge tomb filled with coffins. At the intersection, where an ash spawn lies in wait, take the western path first and search the knapsack for the [Fort Frostmoth Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth_Key "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth Key") and read through the informative *[Ildari's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal")* that sits on the coffin in the center. It is the journal of a conjurer named [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Lore:Ildari_Sarothril "Lore:Ildari Sarothril") who uncovered the tomb and started experimenting with using heartstones to reanimate the dead bodies of the imperials, including the deceased general Falx Carius. She succeeded but the general slowly became hostile and she had to abandon the experiment.

With the key in hand, return to the first room and unlock the wooden door next to Maximian Axius's skeleton. (though you could also use the key to unlock the gate with the master lock, if you were unsuccessful or found lockpicking it too difficult). Head up the stairs and you will soon spot your target in the distance, Falx Carius himself, reanimated and still fighting to protect Fort Frostmoth, thus sending ash spawn to what he believes are enemies living in Raven Rock. If fought toe to toe, he is a very powerful foe and won't go down easily, nor will the ash spawn minions around him. Sadly, none of General Carius' armor can be looted, but claiming his unique enchanted warhammer [Champion's Cudgel](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Cudgel "Skyrim:Champion's Cudgel") should serve as a consolation prize, along with the large chest nearby. Afterwards, leave Fort Frostmoth via the ladder to the south.

### The Reward

Back in Raven Rock, Captain Veleth will have picked up his usual routines but will be eager to hear news from Fort Frostmoth. When you tell him that you killed the reanimated General Falx Carius he will be pleasantly surprised: *"I had my suspicions that he was undead. How else could he have survived for over 200 years? It's a shame. There are quite a few tales of General Carius's exploits, including the founding of Raven Rock. Councilor Morvayn told me to give this to you if you made it back in one piece... and you got rid of General Carius."* He will then hand you a leveled amount of gold as reward. Once you have completed this quest and [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent"), Captain Veleth will have another task ready for you, namely the quest [Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold").

### Reward

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1-29 | 1,500 |
| 30-39 | 2,500 |
| 40-49 | 5,000 |
| 50-59 | 7,500 |
| 60+ | 10,000 |

## Notes

- When you start the quest and don't go to Fort Frostmoth right away, ash spawn will attack Raven Rock. They will keep attacking Raven Rock until you go to Fort Frostmoth.

- General Falx Carius was a character from the [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon") expansion of [Morrowind](/wiki/Morrowind:Morrowind "Morrowind:Morrowind"). See the [Lore article](/wiki/Lore:Falx_Carius "Lore:Falx Carius") for the full story.

- You will encounter [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril") during the quest [Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends").

- If you have killed General Carius before starting or progressing the quest to stage 40, then retrieving a letter [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Imperial_City "Skyrim:Letter to Imperial City") from his corpse and turning it in to Captain Veleth will also lead to quest completion.

## Bugs

- This quest may fail to load entirely on the Anniversary Edition on Nintendo Switch.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.1.392.392534.8, fixes this bug.
- Bypassing the first three ash spawn encountered at the beginning and going directly to Fort Frostmoth to finish the quest may make the three ash spawn in the beginning impervious to any damage or effects.
  -  Open the console, select an ash spawn, and use the code `ToggleActorsAI` followed by `Disable`. Once this has been done to all 3 spawn, they should be gone the next time you enter the cell.
- If you don't search the ash piles from the defeated ash spawn and instead leave to do something else, the ash piles will be gone when you return and you will be unable to progress further in the quest.

A fix to this is to go through the main entrance of Fort Frostmoth, pick the Master Lock in the basement jail cell with the Wax Key perk. You will now have a copy of the Fort Frostmoth key. You can then kill General Falx Carius and return to Captain Veleth.

- -  The note can be added via the console command `player.additem xx01bfe5 1`, where `xx` varies depending on load order. (For example, if Dragonborn.esm is fifth from the top of the load order, the appropriate command would be `player.additem 0501bfe5 1`)
- Even after you finish the quest, ash spawn can continue to attack Raven Rock. **?**

| March of the Dead (DLC2RR01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 30 |  | I've stumbled across a dark elf in combat for his life with strange, ashen beings at the Attius Farm outside of Raven Rock. He appears outnumbered, and he's requested I lend him a helping hand. *Objective 10:* Kill the ash spawn attacking Captain Veleth |
| 40 |  | I've stumbled across Captain Modyn Veleth fighting strange beings called "ash spawn" at the Attius Farm outside of Raven Rock. Captain Veleth was outnumbered, so I engaged his attackers and lent him a helping hand. *Objective 20:* Speak to Captain Veleth |
| 50 |  | Captain Veleth explained that the ash spawn have been attacking Raven Rock for some time now, and he's been trying to locate their source. His lack of manpower and reluctance to leave the town without a commander are keeping him from finding out more. As a result of our conversation, I've agreed to help him deal with this situation. I need to begin by searching the Attius Farm for clues that might lead me to the ash spawn's source. *Objective 30:* Search the Attius Farm for clues |
| 60 |  | While assisting Captain Veleth at the Attius Farm, I've discovered a strange note. I should give this note to Captain Veleth in order to learn more about the origins of the ash spawn threat to Raven Rock. *Objective 50:* Give the note to Captain Veleth |
| 80 |  | Captain Veleth was alarmed by the strange note I recovered from the ash spawn at the Attius Farm. The note mentions Fort Frostmoth, the ruins of an Imperial fort located southeast of Raven Rock. According to him, the fort's been abandoned ever since the eruption of Red Mountain. He's sent me to Fort Frostmoth to kill the author of the note, General Falx Carius, before the town falls prey to his threats. *Objective 60:* Kill General Falx Carius |
| 90 |  | I've slain General Falx Carius in the ruins of Fort Frostmoth and put an end to any further ash spawn attacking Raven Rock. I should return to Captain Modyn Veleth and inform him of my victory. *Objective 70:* Return to Captain Veleth |
| 100 |  | I've slain General Falx Carius in the ruins of Fort Frostmoth. I should examine his remains to determine what he was doing here. *Objective 80:* Search General Carius's remains |
| 110 |  | *Objective 90:* Read the note |
| 120 |  | According to the letter I found on General Carius's remains, he appeared to be responsible for sending what he calls his "men" to attack the town of Raven Rock. I should bring this information to the guards in Raven Rock and let them know the threat has been eliminated. *Objective 100:* Bring the note to a guard in Raven Rock |
| 130 |  | *Objective 110:* Give the note to Captain Veleth |
| 200 | ☑ | I've slain General Falx Carius in the ruins of Fort Frostmoth and put an end to any further ash spawn attacking Raven Rock. Captain Veleth was very pleased with my results, and awarded me a bounty in gold. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 20, 45.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RR01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RR01`.

Marise Aravel's House

**Marise Aravel's House** is a house located on the lower level in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). It is found down by the canal that flows through the middle of Riften and is the first house on the left when coming from [Elgrim's Elixirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Elgrim%27s_Elixirs "Skyrim:Elgrim's Elixirs"). Below the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara"), and east of the entrance to [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Marise Aravel](/wiki/Skyrim:Marise_Aravel "Skyrim:Marise Aravel") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink") |

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Marise Aravel's House

Marise Aravel's home

The front door is apprentice-locked both at night and during the day while Marise is selling [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") at her cart by the marketplace. Her home is one room divided by a partial wall. The main living area consists of a central dining table and benches. On the table is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"). Against the east wall, opposite the entrance is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") to the right.

On the south wall is a shelf holding a bottle of wine with two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") all hanging above the shelf. Against the partial north wall is a dresser and a set of shelves. On the shelves are two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a couple of loaves of bread and several pieces of cheese. On top of these shelves contained in a basket is a copy of the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Reality & Other Falsehoods](/wiki/Skyrim:Reality_%26_Other_Falsehoods "Skyrim:Reality & Other Falsehoods")*. While above the wall are a couple of hanging racks that hold two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). There are sacks and barrels all containing foodstuffs all around the room.

To the north is her bedroom area, which consists of an owned single bed coming out from the east wall with several crates, sacks and an end table beside it. Under the bed is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). On the end table is a bottle of wine and a copy of *[Watcher of Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Watcher_of_Stones "Skyrim:Watcher of Stones")*. On one of the crates is a copy of *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*. There is a wardrobe against the north wall containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") along with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and food barrel against the west wall.

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") on the right door step. There is a chest with minor loot inside.

## Bugs

- Magelight will disappear if it hits the middle wall, but can land on the floors, ceiling, and outer walls just fine. An already existing magelight continues to exist when a new cast is deleted by the wall. **?**

[‡](#note_Ghorza)Ghorza gra-Bagol only offers services at the forge located outside the Castle Markarth proper (just north of The Hag's Cure).

[^a](#note_dieToD)These people can die as part of the [Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") quest.

[^b](#note_dieFC)These people can die as part of the [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") quest.

[^c](#note_dieNOECM)These people can die as part of the [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") quest.

[^d](#note_dieEnter)These people can die when you first enter the city.

[^e](#note_dieHoH)Vigilant Tyranus can die as part of the [House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors") quest.

[^f](#note_Banning)Banning is not a potential follower, but will sell the canine follower Vigilance.

[^g](#note_Fjotra)Fjotra only appears after the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella").

## Overview

The Markarth Stables

**Markarth Stables** is a [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") located outside [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), opposite the entrance.

A black and white [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") may be purchased here for 1000 [Septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") from [Cedran](/wiki/Skyrim:Cedran "Skyrim:Cedran") and a war [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") named [Vigilance](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilance "Skyrim:Vigilance") for 500 septims from [Banning](/wiki/Skyrim:Banning "Skyrim:Banning"). They both live at the stables along with Vigilance unless you have bought him.

## Related Quests

- **[Horse Whisperer](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Whisperer "Skyrim:Horse Whisperer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Wild_Horses "Skyrim:Wild Horses"): Purchase a map that lets you find wild horses.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Banning](/wiki/Skyrim:Banning "Skyrim:Banning") [Dog Breeder](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Dog Breeder")  [Cedran](/wiki/Skyrim:Cedran "Skyrim:Cedran") [Hostler](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Hostler")  [Kibell](/wiki/Skyrim:Kibell "Skyrim:Kibell") [Carriage Service](/wiki/Skyrim:Carriage "Carriage Service")  [Vigilance](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilance "Skyrim:Vigilance") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

### Exterior

There is a row of pillars in front of the building supporting a stone porch area where the horses that are for sale are kept, there are several bales of straw for them to used for bedding. To the northwest and also behind the building to the northeast are two [Juniper Berry Trees](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") and to the southeast is a lookout tower manned by a [Markarth Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth Guard") with flights of stairs leading up to it. During the day one or both of [Cedran](/wiki/Skyrim:Cedran "Skyrim:Cedran") and [Banning](/wiki/Skyrim:Banning "Skyrim:Banning"), along with [Vigilance](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilance "Skyrim:Vigilance") will be stood leaning against or near the pillars out front. The entrance is normally novice-locked.

| Plants | Animals |
| --- | --- |
| 2 [Juniper Berry Trees](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") | [Vigilance](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilance "Skyrim:Vigilance")  2 [Horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") |

### Markarth Stables

Through the door is a flight of stairs down to the east. There are stone shelves on either side at the bottom with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a bucket containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") on top of the shelf on the left and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") is on top of the shelf to the right. There is a doorway in front of you leading into the single-roomed dwelling. There is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") on a block of wood on the left and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand beside the north wall, with a leather strip on a shelf beside that. To the right, still against the north wall is a bucket containing a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and a kettle further to the right against the same wall containing two cabbages and a potato, with a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot") and two potatoes (one in a basket) on a wall shelf on the north wall.

Coming out from the same wall is a long wooden table with two chairs. On the table is a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and several pieces of cheese. To the east there is a large wall shelf above several bales of straw with a three [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and a basket containing two cabbages and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). To the south is a raised section with three stairs up to two owned single beds. To the right of the stairs is a round wooden table and chair, with two loaves of bread and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") on top of the table, a food sack on top of a crate beside it on one side and a mead barrel on the floor of the raised section on the other side. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on the raised section between the table and wall. One of the beds is along the east wall, while the other is along the south wall. On a wall shelf by the first bed is the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), with a Crate above the headboard with an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on top and a food sack and leather strip on a block of wood beside the crate and another food sack with a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") on another crate by the foot of the bed. There is a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") under the second bed.

## Notes

- Once you have completed a delivery for Banning you may freely take most items from inside the Stables. If you have also completed the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") to his satisfaction, you can even break in and use [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") to break into the strongbox and take all the gold and Banning will not complain or accuse you of trespassing or stealing.
- If either Cedran or Banning dies - either can die during a dragon attack, or Banning can die in [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") if the player chooses to turn against the dinner guests - then the survivor will NOT take over his mate's services: you cannot end up buying a dog from Cedran or a horse from Banning.

## Bugs

- The player horse here has an improper enable parent setting that can interfere with Civil War handling.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. The enable parent setting on the horse has been removed.

# Skyrim:Markarth

## Overview

|  |  |  |

Markarth, viewed from outside the city gates

Inside Markarth

**Markarth** is a major city in the southwest of Skyrim near the border of [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), and the capital of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). It is housed in an ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") city, making its architecture noticeably different from that of most cities in Skyrim, with much of the city carved into the surrounding rock. [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the initial ruler of the Reach, is having issues with a group known as the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), who infest the nearby countryside and attack travelers on sight. Though many races populate the city, the people of Markarth are not fond of outsiders, and the guards treat them with hostility and suspicion.

Half the city is owned by the Silver-Blood family. The [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") near the entrance to the city is a good place for brawling, picking up bounty letters, hiring a follower, or renting a room. The Silver-Bloods also own [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), which is inside the city walls and used as a prison, said to be the most secure prison in Skyrim. Most of the poor of Markarth live in extreme poverty in an area dug into the cliff called [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"). Many in the Warrens work in the mine and at the smelters in the area. Several shops are in an open-air marketplace near the city entrance. The guards are quartered in a Dwemer dormitory carved out of the stone beneath the imposing [Guard Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Tower "Skyrim:Guard Tower") at the center of the city. Markarth also houses [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), the ancient Dwemer castle and seat of government carved into the mountain at the west end of the city.

For more information on Markarth, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Markarth "Lore:Markarth").

[†](#note_MarkarthStall)These people only sell goods at the market.

[‡](#note_Ghorza)Ghorza gra-Bagol only offers services at the forge located outside the Castle Markarth proper (just north of The Hag's Cure).

[^a](#note_dieToD)These people can die as part of the [Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") quest.

[^b](#note_dieFC)These people can die as part of the [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") quest.

[^c](#note_dieNOECM)These people can die as part of the [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") quest.

[^d](#note_dieEnter)These people can die when you first enter the city.

[^e](#note_dieHoH)Vigilant Tyranus can die as part of the [House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors") quest.

[^f](#note_Banning)Banning is not a potential follower, but will sell the canine follower Vigilance.

[^g](#note_Fjotra)Fjotra only appears after the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella").

#### Daedric

- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

#### Side Quests

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!
- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in Markarth to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

#### Creation Club

- **[Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor"): Investigate rumors of a ghost that haunts the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").
- **[If I had a Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:If_I_had_a_Hammer "Skyrim:If I had a Hammer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer"): Steal a legendary hammer of the gods.
- **[Mightier than the Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Mightier_than_the_Sword "Skyrim:Mightier than the Sword")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Track down some Dwarven loot and beat the competition.
- **[My Pet Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab"): Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").

## Notes

- [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 gold.
- Evidence of the former Dwemer presence in Markarth is found in the deserted ruins of a Dwemer city. The ruins still contain several operational (and hostile) Dwemer machines.
- Markarth is a unique city in that many citizens may be killed depending on the choices that you make during quests, making the phrase that only "Blood and Silver" runs through Markarth true. See the notes to the [table of NPCs above](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth#Markarth_People "Skyrim:Markarth") for details.
- Investing in the various shops here also adds the investment bonuses to your spouse's gold for their shop.
- Markarth also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")* as [Markarth Side](/wiki/Arena:Markarth_Side "Arena:Markarth Side"), and reappears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Markarth "Online:Markarth").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") and [Tacitus Sallustius](/wiki/Skyrim:Tacitus_Sallustius "Skyrim:Tacitus Sallustius")'s conversation only takes place between 9am~8pm, and it isn't affected whether the player has entered the related area.

## Bugs

- There is a dialogue bug with [Markarth guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard") that occurs after the two Forsworn quests. They will attempt to arrest you, and if you reply with any option other than resist arrest, the dialogue will repeat endlessly. **?**
  - The simplest way of resolving this is to go back to the Temple of Talos and speak with the guards inside. Choose the option to go to jail, then walk outside and speak to another guard to pay your bounty, persuade, etc. successfully.
  - For various other methods on how to resolve this, see the [talk page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Markarth "Skyrim talk:Markarth").
- The steward [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") may refuse to speak with you, or will not offer to sell you [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall"). See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall#Bugs "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") for details. **?**

| - [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine") - [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") |

Markarth, viewed from outside the city gates

Inside Markarth

**Markarth** is a major city in the southwest of Skyrim near the border of [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), and the capital of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). It is housed in an ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") city, making its architecture noticeably different from that of most cities in Skyrim, with much of the city carved into the surrounding rock. [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the initial ruler of the Reach, is having issues with a group known as the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), who infest the nearby countryside and attack travelers on sight. Though many races populate the city, the people of Markarth are not fond of outsiders, and the guards treat them with hostility and suspicion.

Half the city is owned by the Silver-Blood family. The [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") near the entrance to the city is a good place for brawling, picking up bounty letters, hiring a follower, or renting a room. The Silver-Bloods also own [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), which is inside the city walls and used as a prison, said to be the most secure prison in Skyrim. Most of the poor of Markarth live in extreme poverty in an area dug into the cliff called [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"). Many in the Warrens work in the mine and at the smelters in the area. Several shops are in an open-air marketplace near the city entrance. The guards are quartered in a Dwemer dormitory carved out of the stone beneath the imposing [Guard Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Tower "Skyrim:Guard Tower") at the center of the city. Markarth also houses [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), the ancient Dwemer castle and seat of government carved into the mountain at the west end of the city.

For more information on Markarth, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Markarth "Lore:Markarth").

[†](#note_MarkarthStall)These people only sell goods at the market.

[‡](#note_Ghorza)Ghorza gra-Bagol only offers services at the forge located outside the Castle Markarth proper (just north of The Hag's Cure).

[^a](#note_dieToD)These people can die as part of the [Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") quest.

[^b](#note_dieFC)These people can die as part of the [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") quest.

[^c](#note_dieNOECM)These people can die as part of the [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") quest.

[^d](#note_dieEnter)These people can die when you first enter the city.

[^e](#note_dieHoH)Vigilant Tyranus can die as part of the [House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors") quest.

[^f](#note_Banning)Banning is not a potential follower, but will sell the canine follower Vigilance.

[^g](#note_Fjotra)Fjotra only appears after the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella").

#### Daedric

- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

#### Side Quests

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!
- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in Markarth to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

| [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") | [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol") | **[Coated in Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Coated_in_Blood "Skyrim:Coated in Blood")**: Bring a [Daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") to [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol"). | - Bring a Daedra's Heart to Moth |  |

#### Creation Club

- **[Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor"): Investigate rumors of a ghost that haunts the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").
- **[If I had a Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:If_I_had_a_Hammer "Skyrim:If I had a Hammer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer"): Steal a legendary hammer of the gods.
- **[Mightier than the Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Mightier_than_the_Sword "Skyrim:Mightier than the Sword")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Track down some Dwarven loot and beat the competition.
- **[My Pet Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab"): Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").

## Notes

- [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 gold.
- Evidence of the former Dwemer presence in Markarth is found in the deserted ruins of a Dwemer city. The ruins still contain several operational (and hostile) Dwemer machines.
- Markarth is a unique city in that many citizens may be killed depending on the choices that you make during quests, making the phrase that only "Blood and Silver" runs through Markarth true. See the notes to the [table of NPCs above](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth#Markarth_People "Skyrim:Markarth") for details.
- Investing in the various shops here also adds the investment bonuses to your spouse's gold for their shop.
- Markarth also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")* as [Markarth Side](/wiki/Arena:Markarth_Side "Arena:Markarth Side"), and reappears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Markarth "Online:Markarth").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") and [Tacitus Sallustius](/wiki/Skyrim:Tacitus_Sallustius "Skyrim:Tacitus Sallustius")'s conversation only takes place between 9am~8pm, and it isn't affected whether the player has entered the related area.

## Bugs

- There is a dialogue bug with [Markarth guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard") that occurs after the two Forsworn quests. They will attempt to arrest you, and if you reply with any option other than resist arrest, the dialogue will repeat endlessly. **?**
  - The simplest way of resolving this is to go back to the Temple of Talos and speak with the guards inside. Choose the option to go to jail, then walk outside and speak to another guard to pay your bounty, persuade, etc. successfully.
  - For various other methods on how to resolve this, see the [talk page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Markarth "Skyrim talk:Markarth").
- The steward [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") may refuse to speak with you, or will not offer to sell you [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall"). See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall#Bugs "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") for details. **?**

Markarth, viewed from outside the city gates

Inside Markarth

**Markarth** is a major city in the southwest of Skyrim near the border of [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), and the capital of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). It is housed in an ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") city, making its architecture noticeably different from that of most cities in Skyrim, with much of the city carved into the surrounding rock. [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the initial ruler of the Reach, is having issues with a group known as the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), who infest the nearby countryside and attack travelers on sight. Though many races populate the city, the people of Markarth are not fond of outsiders, and the guards treat them with hostility and suspicion.

Half the city is owned by the Silver-Blood family. The [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") near the entrance to the city is a good place for brawling, picking up bounty letters, hiring a follower, or renting a room. The Silver-Bloods also own [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), which is inside the city walls and used as a prison, said to be the most secure prison in Skyrim. Most of the poor of Markarth live in extreme poverty in an area dug into the cliff called [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"). Many in the Warrens work in the mine and at the smelters in the area. Several shops are in an open-air marketplace near the city entrance. The guards are quartered in a Dwemer dormitory carved out of the stone beneath the imposing [Guard Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Tower "Skyrim:Guard Tower") at the center of the city. Markarth also houses [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), the ancient Dwemer castle and seat of government carved into the mountain at the west end of the city.

For more information on Markarth, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Markarth "Lore:Markarth").

[†](#note_MarkarthStall)These people only sell goods at the market.

[‡](#note_Ghorza)Ghorza gra-Bagol only offers services at the forge located outside the Castle Markarth proper (just north of The Hag's Cure).

[^a](#note_dieToD)These people can die as part of the [Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") quest.

[^b](#note_dieFC)These people can die as part of the [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") quest.

[^c](#note_dieNOECM)These people can die as part of the [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") quest.

[^d](#note_dieEnter)These people can die when you first enter the city.

[^e](#note_dieHoH)Vigilant Tyranus can die as part of the [House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors") quest.

[^f](#note_Banning)Banning is not a potential follower, but will sell the canine follower Vigilance.

[^g](#note_Fjotra)Fjotra only appears after the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella").

#### Daedric

- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

#### Side Quests

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!
- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in Markarth to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

#### Creation Club

- **[Crypt of the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Crypt_of_the_Heart "Skyrim:Crypt of the Heart")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Knight_Armor "Skyrim:Spell Knight Armor"): Investigate rumors of a ghost that haunts the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").
- **[If I had a Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:If_I_had_a_Hammer "Skyrim:If I had a Hammer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer"): Steal a legendary hammer of the gods.
- **[Mightier than the Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Mightier_than_the_Sword "Skyrim:Mightier than the Sword")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Track down some Dwarven loot and beat the competition.
- **[My Pet Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab"): Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").

## Notes

- [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 gold.
- Evidence of the former Dwemer presence in Markarth is found in the deserted ruins of a Dwemer city. The ruins still contain several operational (and hostile) Dwemer machines.
- Markarth is a unique city in that many citizens may be killed depending on the choices that you make during quests, making the phrase that only "Blood and Silver" runs through Markarth true. See the notes to the [table of NPCs above](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth#Markarth_People "Skyrim:Markarth") for details.
- Investing in the various shops here also adds the investment bonuses to your spouse's gold for their shop.
- Markarth also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")* as [Markarth Side](/wiki/Arena:Markarth_Side "Arena:Markarth Side"), and reappears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Markarth "Online:Markarth").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") and [Tacitus Sallustius](/wiki/Skyrim:Tacitus_Sallustius "Skyrim:Tacitus Sallustius")'s conversation only takes place between 9am~8pm, and it isn't affected whether the player has entered the related area.

## Bugs

- There is a dialogue bug with [Markarth guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard") that occurs after the two Forsworn quests. They will attempt to arrest you, and if you reply with any option other than resist arrest, the dialogue will repeat endlessly. **?**
  - The simplest way of resolving this is to go back to the Temple of Talos and speak with the guards inside. Choose the option to go to jail, then walk outside and speak to another guard to pay your bounty, persuade, etc. successfully.
  - For various other methods on how to resolve this, see the [talk page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Markarth "Skyrim talk:Markarth").
- The steward [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") may refuse to speak with you, or will not offer to sell you [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall"). See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall#Bugs "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") for details. **?**

Markarth, viewed from outside the city gates

Inside Markarth

**Markarth** is a major city in the southwest of Skyrim near the border of [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock"), and the capital of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"). It is housed in an ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") city, making its architecture noticeably different from that of most cities in Skyrim, with much of the city carved into the surrounding rock. [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the initial ruler of the Reach, is having issues with a group known as the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), who infest the nearby countryside and attack travelers on sight. Though many races populate the city, the people of Markarth are not fond of outsiders, and the guards treat them with hostility and suspicion.

Half the city is owned by the Silver-Blood family. The [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") near the entrance to the city is a good place for brawling, picking up bounty letters, hiring a follower, or renting a room. The Silver-Bloods also own [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), which is inside the city walls and used as a prison, said to be the most secure prison in Skyrim. Most of the poor of Markarth live in extreme poverty in an area dug into the cliff called [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"). Many in the Warrens work in the mine and at the smelters in the area. Several shops are in an open-air marketplace near the city entrance. The guards are quartered in a Dwemer dormitory carved out of the stone beneath the imposing [Guard Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Tower "Skyrim:Guard Tower") at the center of the city. Markarth also houses [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), the ancient Dwemer castle and seat of government carved into the mountain at the west end of the city.

For more information on Markarth, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Markarth "Lore:Markarth").

[†](#note_MarkarthStall)These people only sell goods at the market.

[‡](#note_Ghorza)Ghorza gra-Bagol only offers services at the forge located outside the Castle Markarth proper (just north of The Hag's Cure).

[^a](#note_dieToD)These people can die as part of the [Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") quest.

[^b](#note_dieFC)These people can die as part of the [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") quest.

[^c](#note_dieNOECM)These people can die as part of the [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") quest.

[^d](#note_dieEnter)These people can die when you first enter the city.

[^e](#note_dieHoH)Vigilant Tyranus can die as part of the [House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors") quest.

[^f](#note_Banning)Banning is not a potential follower, but will sell the canine follower Vigilance.

[^g](#note_Fjotra)Fjotra only appears after the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella").

#### Daedric

- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

#### Side Quests

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!
- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in Markarth to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

- **[If I had a Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:If_I_had_a_Hammer "Skyrim:If I had a Hammer")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Hammer "Skyrim:Stendarr's Hammer"): Steal a legendary hammer of the gods.
- **[Mightier than the Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Mightier_than_the_Sword "Skyrim:Mightier than the Sword")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Orcish_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Orcish Plate"): Track down some Dwarven loot and beat the competition.
- **[My Pet Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab"): Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").

## Notes

- [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") is a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses") available for purchase after completion of certain quests for the jarl. It may be purchased from the steward for 8,000 gold.
- Evidence of the former Dwemer presence in Markarth is found in the deserted ruins of a Dwemer city. The ruins still contain several operational (and hostile) Dwemer machines.
- Markarth is a unique city in that many citizens may be killed depending on the choices that you make during quests, making the phrase that only "Blood and Silver" runs through Markarth true. See the notes to the [table of NPCs above](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth#Markarth_People "Skyrim:Markarth") for details.
- Investing in the various shops here also adds the investment bonuses to your spouse's gold for their shop.
- Markarth also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")* as [Markarth Side](/wiki/Arena:Markarth_Side "Arena:Markarth Side"), and reappears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Markarth "Online:Markarth").
- There is an initial conversation scene may be missed. [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") and [Tacitus Sallustius](/wiki/Skyrim:Tacitus_Sallustius "Skyrim:Tacitus Sallustius")'s conversation only takes place between 9am~8pm, and it isn't affected whether the player has entered the related area.

## Bugs

- There is a dialogue bug with [Markarth guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard") that occurs after the two Forsworn quests. They will attempt to arrest you, and if you reply with any option other than resist arrest, the dialogue will repeat endlessly. **?**
  - The simplest way of resolving this is to go back to the Temple of Talos and speak with the guards inside. Choose the option to go to jail, then walk outside and speak to another guard to pay your bounty, persuade, etc. successfully.
  - For various other methods on how to resolve this, see the [talk page](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Markarth "Skyrim talk:Markarth").
- The steward [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek") may refuse to speak with you, or will not offer to sell you [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall"). See [this section](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall#Bugs "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") for details. **?**

# Skyrim:Mauhulakh's Longhouse

## Overview

[Mauhulakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Mauhulakh "Skyrim:Chief Mauhulakh")'s Longhouse

**Mauhulakh's Longhouse** is the longhouse of [Chief Mauhulakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Mauhulakh "Skyrim:Chief Mauhulakh"), located in the Orc stronghold of [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur").

The longhouse contains two zones: *[Mauhulakh's Longhouse](#Mauhulakh.27s_Longhouse)* and *[Mauhulakh's Cellar](#Mauhulakh.27s_Cellar)*.

The longhouse is home to [Chief Mauhulakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Mauhulakh "Skyrim:Chief Mauhulakh") and his aunts and children.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Chief Mauhulakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Mauhulakh "Skyrim:Chief Mauhulakh")  [Bolar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar "Skyrim:Bolar") [Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary")  [Dushnamub](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnamub "Skyrim:Dushnamub") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")  [Urog](/wiki/Skyrim:Urog "Skyrim:Urog")  [Yatul](/wiki/Skyrim:Yatul "Skyrim:Yatul") |

### Mauhulakh's Longhouse

The longhouse

It's a typical Orc longhouse with a central room for cooking and eating with wings at either end for sleeping. There is a large fireplace opposite the entrance with a three pots hanging over it, none of them usable as a cooking pot. The middle pot contains two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"). To the left is a long wooden table that has a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") in a bowl on top, while in a basket underneath are two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Hanging above is another leg of goat, a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), a garlic braid, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the left of the table is a set of shelves holding mostly clutter with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). There are two dining tables in the room, one on your left as you enter is set for four and holds two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of Nord mead and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") in a tankard. The second table is to the right of the fireplace and is set for two and holds a rock warbler egg, a bottle of Nord mead and also has a purple mountain flower in a tankard. In the southeast corner is a set of shelves holding two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), three common books, a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and a set of clothes.

The wing to the northwest contains four single beds, two against each wall and is where [Chief Mauhulakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Mauhulakh "Skyrim:Chief Mauhulakh") sleeps along with his children [Dushnamub](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnamub "Skyrim:Dushnamub") and [Urog](/wiki/Skyrim:Urog "Skyrim:Urog"). The room contains an end table, a dresser with a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") on top, a master-locked chest and at the end a pile of sacks and barrels mostly containing food, except one barrel that contains [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and has a common book on top. The southern wing contains a double bed where [Bolar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolar "Skyrim:Bolar") sleeps, with an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") leaning against the side of the bed. In this room, there is an end table, a dresser, an adept-locked chest, and a small set of shelves holding copies of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Knights of the Nine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Knights_of_the_Nine "Skyrim:The Knights of the Nine")*, *[The True Nature of Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Nature_of_Orcs "Skyrim:The True Nature of Orcs")* and *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")* along with a bottle each of alto wine and wine. There is also a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") leaning against these shelves. On top of the dresser, there is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

### Mauhulakh's Cellar

The cellar

Despite lying below the longhouse, this area must be entered from outside. It is a small room with several sets of shelves against the walls. These hold a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), three baskets containing [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), tomatoes and red and green apples, four sheaves of wheat, twenty-three bottles of Nord mead, a kettle containing a bottle of [weak aversion to fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Aversion_to_Fire "Skyrim:Weak Aversion to Fire"), a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide"), a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[Song Of Hrormir](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_Of_Hrormir "Skyrim:Song Of Hrormir")* and a chest with a leveled lock.

## Bugs

- [Yatul](/wiki/Skyrim:Yatul "Skyrim:Yatul") doesn't sleep due to a bug. See [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Yatul#Bugs "Skyrim:Yatul") for details.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Meeko's Shack

## Overview

Meeko's Shack

**Meeko's Shack** is a run-down [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") owned by the canine follower [Meeko](/wiki/Skyrim:Meeko "Skyrim:Meeko"), who has inherited the home from his unfortunate [owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead)#Nord1 "Skyrim:Nord (dead)").

It is located on the edge of the [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") marshland between [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), a short distance from the road leading from Morthal and [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge").

## Meeko's Shack

.jpg)

Meeko's former owner

Around the shack are several plants and flowers including three [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants, a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") and three [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower").

The shack is still fairly structurally sound. Inside there is a small set of shelves to the left of the doorway with a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top. Beside this, in the northern corner is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel with a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v6 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v6")* on top. Against the northeast wall is a set of shelves holding a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a bowl containing three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"). To the right of this is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit"). Against the southeast wall is an unowned single bed with the corpse of [Meeko's](/wiki/Skyrim:Meeko "Skyrim:Meeko") former [owner](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead)#Nord1 "Skyrim:Nord (dead)") laying on top. It can still be used to rest. At the foot of the bed is an end table with a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_(Meeko%27s_Shack) "Skyrim:Journal (Meeko's Shack)") written by Meeko's former owner. It explains that he had succumbed to [Rockjoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Disease "Skyrim:Disease") and that Meeko "was always a loyal companion" and would "be able to take care of himself".

## Notes

- Meeko runs back to the shack if you find him on the road.
- There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") to the northwest.
- A [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") can be found to the west of the shack.
- While technically owned by Meeko, none of the items inside the shack are owned and will not be marked as stolen should you take them.
- After you have discovered Meeko and his dead master, the body and bed will be disposed of automatically upon the next cell reset.
